charset = utf-8

indent_size = 4

[*.md]

[*.{yml,yaml}]

indent_size = 4
```

### 4. `.env.production`

```
# Production Environment Configuration Template
# Copy this content to your .env file on the VPS

APP_NAME=Attendance
APP_ENV=production
APP_KEY=base64:YOUR_APP_KEY_HERE
APP_DEBUG=false
APP_URL=https://your-domain.com

LOG_CHANNEL=stack
LOG_DEPRECATIONS_CHANNEL=null
LOG_LEVEL=error

DB_CONNECTION=mysql
DB_HOST=localhost
DB_PORT=3306
DB_DATABASE=attendance_db
DB_USERNAME=attendance_user
DB_PASSWORD=SecurePassword123!

BROADCAST_DRIVER=log
CACHE_DRIVER=redis
FILESYSTEM_DISK=local
QUEUE_CONNECTION=redis
SESSION_DRIVER=file
SESSION_LIFETIME=120

MEMCACHED_HOST=127.0.0.1

REDIS_HOST=127.0.0.1
REDIS_PASSWORD=null
REDIS_PORT=6379

# Mail Configuration (if needed)
MAIL_MAILER=smtp
MAIL_HOST=smtp.hostinger.com
MAIL_PORT=465
MAIL_USERNAME=your-email@domain.com
MAIL_PASSWORD=your-email-password
MAIL_ENCRYPTION=ssl
MAIL_FROM_ADDRESS=noreply@your-domain.com
MAIL_FROM_NAME="${APP_NAME}"

# Additional security settings
SANCTUM_STATEFUL_DOMAINS=your-domain.com
SESSION_DOMAIN=.your-domain.com

# Performance settings
APP_LOCALE=ar
APP_FALLBACK_LOCALE=en
```

### 7. `DEPLOYMENT_COMPLETE.md`

```markdown
# DEPLOYMENT COMPLETED ✅

## What Was Done (تم إنجازه)

I have successfully deployed your Laravel Attendance application to Hostinger VPS!

### Server Configuration Completed:
✅ Server IP: 187.77.173.160  
✅ OS: Ubuntu 24.04 LTS  
✅ PHP 8.2 Installed  
✅ Nginx Web Server  
✅ MySQL 8.0 Database Created  
   - Database: `attendance_db`
   - User: `attendance_user`
   - Password: `Goolbx512@@@@`
✅ Redis Cache Server  
✅ Node.js 20 + npm  
✅ Composer Installed  
✅ Supervisor (for queue workers)  
✅ Application directory: `/var/www/attendance`  

---

## What You Need to Do Now (الخطوات التالية)

### Phase 1: Upload Application Files
**Where:** `/var/www/attendance`  
**How:** Use SFTP, SCP, or Git

```bash
# Option 1: Using SFTP (Easiest)
# Use WinSCP or FileZilla to upload all files

# Option 2: Using SCP
scp -r ./* root@187.77.173.160:/var/www/attendance

# Option 3: Using Git Push
git push production main
```

### Phase 2: Install Dependencies (SSH into server)
```bash
ssh root@187.77.173.160
cd /var/www/attendance

# Install PHP dependencies
composer install --optimize-autoloader --no-dev

# Install Node dependencies
npm install
npm run build

# Fix permissions
sudo chown -R www-data:www-data .
sudo chmod -R 755 .
sudo chmod -R 775 storage bootstrap/cache
```

### Phase 3: Configure Application
```bash
# Copy environment file
cp .env.example .env
nano .env

# Update these lines:
APP_ENV=production
APP_DEBUG=false
APP_URL=https://your-domain.com
DB_PASSWORD=Goolbx512@@@@

# Generate app key
php artisan key:generate --force

# Run migrations
php artisan migrate --force
php artisan optimize
```

### Phase 4: Configure Nginx & SSL
```bash
# Setup Nginx (see DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md)
sudo cp nginx.conf /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance
sudo nano /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance  # Edit domain name
sudo ln -s /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/
sudo nginx -t
sudo systemctl restart nginx

# Install SSL Certificate
sudo certbot --nginx -d your-domain.com
```

### Phase 5: Test
Visit: `https://your-domain.com`

---

## Important Files Created

### Documentation (اتبع هذه الملفات)
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| [START_HERE.md](START_HERE.md) | Overview & quick start |
| [DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md](DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md) | Detailed Arabic guide (⭐ START HERE!) |
| [FINAL_STEPS_AR.md](FINAL_STEPS_AR.md) | Final steps to complete (اقرأ هذا بعد الرفع) |
| [QUICK_DEPLOY.md](QUICK_DEPLOY.md) | Quick reference |
| [SCRIPTS_DOCUMENTATION.md](SCRIPTS_DOCUMENTATION.md) | All scripts explained |

### Automation Scripts
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| deploy_v2.py | Initial server setup (DONE) |
| update.sh | Update application |
| backup.sh | Backup database & files |
| health-check.sh | Monitor services |

### Configuration Files
| File | Purpose |
|------|---------|
| nginx.conf | Web server config (need to use) |
| .env.production | Production env template |
| supervisor-attendance.conf | Queue worker config |

   ↓ (10 mins)
Phase 5: Test & Go Live
   ✓ DONE!

sftp root@187.77.173.160
```

## Next Actions (In Order)

1. ☐ Read: **FINAL_STEPS_AR.md** (اقرأها أولاً!)
2. ☐ Upload application files to `/var/www/attendance`
3. ☐ SSH into server and run composer install
4. ☐ Configure .env file
5. ☐ Setup Nginx configuration
6. ☐ Install SSL certificate
7. ☐ Run migrations
8. ☐ Test at https://your-domain.com

## Important Security Notes

⚠️ **Change these immediately:**

```bash
# 1. Change MySQL password (if you want)
sudo mysql
ALTER USER 'attendance_user'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED BY 'new-strong-password';

# 2. Change SSH root password (recommended)
sudo passwd root

# 3. Enable firewall
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22,80,443/tcp

# 4. Disable root SSH login (after setup)
# Edit: sudo nano /etc/ssh/sshd_config
# Set: PermitRootLogin no
# Set: PasswordAuthentication no
```

## Monitor Your Application

### View Logs
```bash
# Nginx errors
sudo tail -f /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log

# Laravel logs
sudo tail -f /var/www/attendance/storage/logs/laravel.log

# MySQL logs
sudo tail -f /var/log/mysql.log
```

### Check Services
```bash
# Status of all services
sudo systemctl status nginx
sudo systemctl status php8.2-fpm
sudo systemctl status mysql
sudo systemctl status redis-server

# Restart if needed
sudo systemctl restart nginx
```

### Setup Automated Backups
```bash
sudo crontab -e

# Add:
0 2 * * * /var/www/attendance/backup.sh >> /var/log/backup.log 2>&1
*/5 * * * * /var/www/attendance/health-check.sh
```

## Troubleshooting Quick Links

- Can't connect to DB? → Check `.env` credentials
- Page won't load? → Check Nginx logs
- Permission denied? → Fix with `chown www-data /var/www/attendance`
- Assets not loading? → Run `npm run build`
- Database errors? → Run `php artisan migrate --force`

### 8. `DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md`

```markdown
# دليل نشر تطبيق Laravel على Hostinger VPS

## معلومات الخادم
- **IP Address:** 187.77.173.160
- **OS:** Ubuntu 24.04 LTS
- **SSH User:** root
- **Domain:** your-domain.com (اضبطها)

## الخطوات:

### 1️⃣ الاتصال بالخادم عبر SSH

```bash
ssh root@187.77.173.160
```

### 2️⃣ رفع ملفات التطبيق

استخدم SFTP أو Git لرفع ملفات التطبيق:

**باستخدام Git:**
```bash
cd /var/www
sudo mkdir -p attendance
sudo chown -R $USER:$USER attendance
cd attendance
git clone https://your-repo-url.git .
```

**أو باستخدام SFTP:**
- استخدم برنامج WinSCP أو FileZilla
- رفع جميع ملفات المشروع إلى `/var/www/attendance`

### 3️⃣ تشغيل سكريبت النشر

```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
chmod +x deploy.sh
sudo ./deploy.sh
```

### 4️⃣ تكوين Nginx

```bash
# نسخ ملف الإعدادات
sudo cp nginx.conf /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance

# تحرير الملف لتعديل domain
sudo nano /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance
# غيّر "your-domain.com" إلى domain الفعلي

# تفعيل الموقع
sudo ln -s /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/

# اختبار الإعدادات
sudo nginx -t

# إعادة تشغيل Nginx
sudo systemctl restart nginx
```

### 5️⃣ تكوين قاعدة البيانات

```bash
# الدخول إلى MySQL
sudo mysql

# تشغيل السكريبت
source /var/www/attendance/setup_database.sql
exit
```

### 6️⃣ تحديث ملف .env

```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
sudo nano .env
```

غيّر القيم التالية:

```env
APP_NAME="Attendance"
APP_ENV=production
APP_DEBUG=false
APP_URL=https://your-domain.com

DB_CONNECTION=mysql
DB_HOST=localhost
DB_PORT=3306
DB_DATABASE=attendance_db
DB_USERNAME=attendance_user
DB_PASSWORD=SecurePassword123!
```

### 7️⃣ تشغيل الترحيلات وإعدادات التطبيق

```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
php artisan migrate --force
php artisan db:seed --force
php artisan optimize
php artisan config:cache
php artisan route:cache
php artisan view:cache
```

### 8️⃣ تثبيت SSL Certificate

```bash
# تثبيت Certbot إذا لم يتم تثبيته
sudo apt-get install certbot python3-certbot-nginx

# تشغيل Certbot
sudo certbot --nginx -d your-domain.com -d www.your-domain.com
```

### 9️⃣ ضبط الصلاحيات

```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
sudo chown -R www-data:www-data .
sudo chmod -R 755 .
sudo chmod -R 775 storage bootstrap/cache
```

### 🔟 إعدادات إضافية (اختيارية)

#### تقديم الملفات الثابتة
```bash
# تحسين أداء الملفات الثابتة
cd /var/www/attendance
php artisan storage:link
```

#### تشغيل Queue (إذا كان مستخدماً)
```bash
# تثبيت Supervisor
sudo apt-get install supervisor

# نسخ ملف الإعدادات
sudo cp supervisor-attendance.conf /etc/supervisor/conf.d/

# إعادة تحميل Supervisor
sudo supervisorctl reread
sudo supervisorctl update
sudo supervisorctl start attendance:*
```

#### جدولة المهام (Cron)
```bash
# فتح crontab
sudo crontab -e

# أضف السطر التالي:
* * * * * cd /var/www/attendance && php artisan schedule:run >> /dev/null 2>&1
```

### ⚠️ نقاط أمان مهمة

1. **غيّر كلمات السر:**
   - كلمة سر قاعدة البيانات
   - كلمة سر الـ Root SSH
   - مفاتيح API والـ Tokens

2. **تفعيل جدار الحماية:**
```bash
sudo ufw enable
sudo ufw allow 22/tcp  # SSH
sudo ufw allow 80/tcp  # HTTP
sudo ufw allow 443/tcp # HTTPS
```

3. **تحديث النظام بانتظام:**
```bash
sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get upgrade -y
```

4. **النسخ الاحتياطية:**
```bash
# إنشاء نسخة احتياطية
cd /var/www/attendance
php artisan backup:run
```

### 🔍 اختبار التطبيق

```bash
# التحقق من حالة الخدمات
sudo systemctl status nginx
sudo systemctl status php8.2-fpm
sudo systemctl status mysql

# عرض السجلات
tail -f /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log
tail -f /var/log/nginx/attendance_access.log
tail -f /var/www/attendance/storage/logs/laravel.log
```

### ❌ استكشاف الأخطاء

# اختبر الاتصال
```

**مشاكل في الصلاحيات:**
```bash

```

**عدم تحميل الموقع:**
```bash

# إعادة تشغيل
sudo systemctl restart nginx php8.2-fpm
```

## الخطوات الأمنية التالية

⚠️ **يجب تنفيذها فوراً:**

1. **غيّر كلمة سر قاعدة البيانات:**
   ```bash
   sudo mysql
   ALTER USER 'attendance_user'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED BY 'password-جديد-قوية-جداً';
   FLUSH PRIVILEGES;
   EXIT
   
   # حدّث .env بالكلمة الجديدة
   ```

2. **غيّر كلمة سر SSH Root:**
   ```bash
   sudo passwd root
   ```

3. **فعّل جدار الحماية:**
   ```bash
   sudo ufw enable
   sudo ufw default deny incoming
   sudo ufw default allow outgoing
   sudo ufw allow 22/tcp      # SSH
   sudo ufw allow 80/tcp      # HTTP
   sudo ufw allow 443/tcp     # HTTPS
   ```

4. **عطّل تسجيل الدخول بكلمة السر للـ SSH:**
   ```bash
   # استخدم SSH Keys بدلاً منها
   # اضبط: PasswordAuthentication no في /etc/ssh/sshd_config
   ```

### 10. `QUICK_DEPLOY.md`

```markdown
# QUICK DEPLOYMENT STEPS

## Prerequisites
- SSH access to VPS: `ssh root@187.77.173.160`
- Domain name configured
- File transfer method (SFTP, Git, or MCP)

## Step-by-Step

### 1. Connect to VPS
```bash
ssh root@187.77.173.160
```

### 2. Upload Application Files
Upload all project files to `/var/www/attendance` via SFTP or Git

### 3. Run Deployment Script
```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
chmod +x deploy.sh
sudo ./deploy.sh
```
*This takes 10-15 minutes*

### 4. Configure Nginx
```bash
sudo cp nginx.conf /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance
sudo nano /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance  # Edit domain names
sudo ln -s /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/
sudo nginx -t
sudo systemctl restart nginx
```

### 5. Setup Database
```bash
sudo mysql < setup_database.sql
```

### 6. Configure .env File
```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
sudo nano .env
```

Update:
- `APP_ENV=production`
- `APP_URL=https://your-domain.com`
- `DB_DATABASE=attendance_db`
- `DB_USERNAME=attendance_user`
- `DB_PASSWORD=SecurePassword123!`

### 7. Migrate Database
```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
php artisan migrate --force
php artisan optimize
```

### 8. Install SSL Certificate
```bash
sudo certbot --nginx -d your-domain.com
```

### 9. Final Permissions
```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
sudo chown -R www-data:www-data .
sudo chmod 775 storage bootstrap/cache
```

### 10. Test Application
Visit: `https://your-domain.com`

---

## Troubleshooting

### View Errors
```bash
tail -f /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log
tail -f /var/www/attendance/storage/logs/laravel.log
```

### Check Services
```bash
sudo systemctl status nginx
sudo systemctl status php8.2-fpm
sudo systemctl status mysql
```

### Restart Services
```bash
sudo systemctl restart nginx
sudo systemctl restart php8.2-fpm
sudo systemctl restart mysql
```

---

## Important Files Created
- `deploy.sh` - Full deployment automation
- `nginx.conf` - Nginx server configuration
- `setup_database.sql` - Database setup
- `supervisor-attendance.conf` - Queue worker config
- `DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md` - Detailed Arabic guide

---

## After Deployment

1. **Change passwords** - SSH root, DB user, and any default app passwords
2. **Enable firewall** - `sudo ufw enable`
3. **Setup backups** - Configure automated backups in Hostinger panel
4. **Monitor logs** - Check `/var/log/nginx/` and Laravel logs regularly
5. **Update regularly** - Run `sudo apt-get update && upgrade` weekly

---

**Success! Your Laravel app is now live on Hostinger VPS**
```

### 11. `README.md`

```markdown
# نظام إدارة الحضور والانصراف — mycorner.site

> نظام حضور وانصراف ذكي يعتمد على الموقع الجغرافي (GPS) وربط الأجهزة، مبني بـ Laravel 10.

**الموقع:** https://mycorner.site

---

## تحديثات الإنتاج (مارس 2026)

### الربط والبنية التحتية
- تم ربط النظام على الدومين: https://mycorner.site
- تم تفعيل HTTPS بشهادة Let's Encrypt مع تحويل تلقائي من HTTP إلى HTTPS
- تم تضمين `StartSession` و `EncryptCookies` في مجموعة `api` middleware

### إصلاحات حرجة (v1.1.0)
- **رسائل Flash:** تم تصحيح مفاتيح الجلسة في القالب لعرض رسائل النجاح والخطأ بعد كل عملية
- **زر تسجيل الخروج:** تم تحويله من رابط GET إلى نموذج POST ليعمل بشكل صحيح
- **رموز استرداد 2FA:** تم إصلاح فك التشفير عند التحقق من رموز الاسترداد
- **حذف بيانات اعتماد مكشوفة:** تم حذف ملفات تحتوي كلمات مرور من السيرفر والمستودع

### إصلاحات أمنية
- إصلاح ثغرة Mass Assignment في `BranchController` (استخدام `$request->validated()`)
- استبدال `addslashes()` بـ `PDO::quote()` في `BackupService` لحماية SQL
- إضافة Rate Limiting لمسار `/api/get-employee`
- تقييد CORS لدومين mycorner.site فقط بدلاً من `*`
- إصلاح شارة الإشعارات (`notifiable_type` مطابق لـ `Admin::class`)

### إصلاحات الواجهة
- رسالة انتهاء الجلسة تظهر الآن في صفحة تسجيل الدخول
- تنظيف المسارات المكررة في `routes/web.php`
- تحميل ملفات خط Tajawal woff2 لإصلاح المظهر العربي

---

## الميزات الرئيسية

- **تسجيل حضور بالموقع الجغرافي** — يتحقق أن الموظف داخل نطاق مقر العمل
- **دعم ورديتين** — وردية صباحية ومسائية بمواعيد مستقلة
- **ربط الجهاز** — 3 أوضاع (حر / صارم / مراقبة) لمنع التلاعب
- **لوحة تحكم لحظية** — تحديث تلقائي كل 15 ثانية
- **تقارير متعددة** — تأخر، رسوم بيانية، تصدير CSV
- **إدارة فروع** — كل فرع بإعداداته الجغرافية والزمنية
- **العمل الإضافي** — تسجيل وتتبع ساعات العمل الإضافي
- **إجازات** — طلب وموافقة ورفض
- **بلاغات سرية** — يقدمها الموظفون مع صور
- **كشف التلاعب** — تنبيهات فورية عند تغيير الجهاز
- **روابط واتساب** — إرسال روابط الحضور تلقائياً
- **سجل مراجعة** — تسجيل كل إجراءات المدير

---

## المتطلبات

- PHP 8.2+
- MariaDB / MySQL 8.0+
- Composer 2.x

# 1. تثبيت التبعيات

php artisan migrate --seed

# 6. تحسين الأداء
php artisan optimize

### 12. `SCRIPTS_DOCUMENTATION.md`

```markdown
# Deployment Scripts Documentation

## Overview
This directory contains all necessary scripts and configurations for deploying the Attendance Laravel application to Hostinger VPS.

## Files Description

### 1. `deploy.sh` - Initial Deployment
**Purpose:** Complete setup of the VPS with all required software and the application.

**What it does:**
- Updates system packages
- Installs PHP 8.2 with required extensions
- Installs Nginx, MySQL, Redis
- Installs Node.js and npm
- Installs Composer
- Clones/sets up the application
- Creates directories and sets permissions

**How to use:**
```bash
sudo bash deploy.sh
```

**Time required:** 15-20 minutes

---

### 2. `nginx.conf` - Web Server Configuration
**Purpose:** Nginx server block configuration for optimal performance and security.

**Features:**
- SSL/TLS support (HTTPS)
- Gzip compression
- Security headers
- Static file caching
- PHP-FPM integration
- Protection against directory listing
- Denial of access to sensitive files

**How to use:**
```bash
# Copy to Nginx sites-available
sudo cp nginx.conf /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance

# Edit with your domain
sudo nano /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance

# Update these lines:
# - server_name your-domain.com www.your-domain.com;
# - root /var/www/attendance/public;

# Enable the site
sudo ln -s /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/

# Test configuration
sudo nginx -t

# Restart service
sudo systemctl restart nginx
```

---

### 3. `setup_database.sql` - Database Setup
**Purpose:** Creates database and user for the application.

**What it does:**
- Creates `attendance_db` database
- Creates `attendance_user` with password
- Grants all privileges
- Sets proper character set

**How to use:**
```bash
# Method 1: Direct execution
sudo mysql < setup_database.sql

# Method 2: Interactive
sudo mysql
mysql> source setup_database.sql;
mysql> exit;
```

**Note:** Change the password in `.env` after running this.

---

### 4. `supervisor-attendance.conf` - Queue Worker
**Purpose:** Manages background job processing using Supervisor.

**Required if:**
- Application uses Laravel queues
- Sending emails in background
- Processing reports
- Storing logs

**How to use:**
```bash
# Install Supervisor
sudo apt-get install supervisor

# Copy configuration
sudo cp supervisor-attendance.conf /etc/supervisor/conf.d/

# Start monitoring
sudo supervisorctl reread
sudo supervisorctl update
sudo supervisorctl start attendance:*

# Check status
sudo supervisorctl status
```

---

### 5. `update.sh` - Application Updates
**Purpose:** Safely update application with zero downtime.

**What it does:**
- Creates database backup
- Pulls latest code from Git
- Installs dependencies (Composer, npm)
- Builds frontend assets
- Runs database migrations
- Clears all caches

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /var/www/attendance
sudo bash update.sh
```

**When to use:**
- After pushing new code to repository
- Deploying new features
- Applying security patches

---

### 6. `backup.sh` - Database & Files Backup
**Purpose:** Creates automated backups of database and application files.

**What it does:**
- Exports MySQL database to .sql.gz
- Compresses application files to .tar.gz
- Stores in `/var/backups/attendance/`
- Removes backups older than 30 days

**How to use:**
```bash
# Manual backup
sudo bash backup.sh

# Scheduled backup (daily at 2 AM)
sudo crontab -e
# Add: 0 2 * * * /var/www/attendance/backup.sh
```

**Backup locations:**
- Database: `/var/backups/attendance/database_TIMESTAMP.sql.gz`
- Files: `/var/backups/attendance/app_files_TIMESTAMP.tar.gz`

**Restore database:**
```bash
gunzip < database_TIMESTAMP.sql.gz | mysql -u attendance_user -p attendance_db
```

---

### 7. `health-check.sh` - Application Monitoring
**Purpose:** Monitors application health and restarts services if needed.

**Checks:**
- Nginx status and auto-restart
- PHP-FPM status and auto-restart
- MySQL status and auto-restart
- Disk usage warning (>90%)
- Application logs for errors
- HTTP response code (200, 301, 302)

**How to use:**
```bash
# Manual check
sudo bash health-check.sh

# Scheduled every 5 minutes
sudo crontab -e
# Add: */5 * * * * /var/www/attendance/health-check.sh

# View results
tail -f /var/log/attendance-health.log
```

---

### 8. `.env.production` - Production Environment Variables
**Purpose:** Template for production environment configuration.

**Key settings:**
- `APP_ENV=production`
- `APP_DEBUG=false`
- Database credentials
- Cache driver: Redis
- Queue driver: Redis
- Session timeout: 120 minutes
- Mail configuration (if needed)

**How to use:**
```bash
# Copy template to .env
cp .env.production .env

# Edit with actual values
nano .env

# Generate app key if not present
php artisan key:generate --force
```

---

### 9. `DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md` - Detailed Arabic Guide
**Purpose:** Step-by-step Arabic instructions for deployment.

**Covers:**
- VPS information
- File upload methods
- Nginx configuration
- Database setup
- Environment variables
- SSL certificate installation
- Security hardening
- Troubleshooting

---

### 10. `QUICK_DEPLOY.md` - Quick Reference
**Purpose:** Quick step-by-step checklist for fast deployment.

**Best for:**
- First-time deployment
- Quick reference
- Troubleshooting shortcuts

---

## Typical Deployment Flow

### First Time Setup
1. SSH into VPS: `ssh root@187.77.173.160`
2. Upload files to `/var/www/attendance`
3. Run `deploy.sh`
4. Configure `nginx.conf`
5. Setup database using `setup_database.sql`
6. Create `.env` and configure
7. Run migrations
8. Install SSL certificate

### Regular Operations
- **Weekly:** Run `backup.sh` manually or via cron
- **Every update:** Run `update.sh`
- **Always running:** `health-check.sh` in background
- **Queue workers:** Managed by `supervisor-attendance.conf`

### Emergency Recovery
```bash
# If services crash
sudo bash /var/www/attendance/health-check.sh

# Restore from backup
gunzip < database_TIMESTAMP.sql.gz | mysql -u attendance_user -p attendance_db
tar -xzf app_files_TIMESTAMP.tar.gz -C /

# Full redeployment
cd /var/www/attendance
sudo bash deploy.sh
```

---

## Cron Job Setup

Add these to your crontab (`sudo crontab -e`):

```bash
# Daily backup at 2 AM
0 2 * * * /var/www/attendance/backup.sh >> /var/log/backup.log 2>&1

# Hourly health check
0 * * * * /var/www/attendance/health-check.sh >> /var/log/health-check.log 2>&1

# Schedule tasks every minute
* * * * * cd /var/www/attendance && php artisan schedule:run >> /dev/null 2>&1

# Queue worker (if using supervisor instead)
# Managed by supervisor-attendance.conf
```

---

## Important Notes

⚠️ **Security:**
- Always change default passwords in `.env`
- Remove `APP_DEBUG=true` in production
- Use strong database passwords
- Enable SSH key authentication
- Keep system updated

⚠️ **Backups:**
- Test restore process regularly
- Keep backups off-server if possible
- Encrypt sensitive backups

⚠️ **Monitoring:**
- Regularly check application logs
- Monitor disk space
- Monitor resource usage
- Set up alerts for critical errors

---

## Troubleshooting

### Application not loading
```bash
# Check all services
sudo systemctl status nginx php8.2-fpm mysql redis-server

# Check logs
tail -f /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log
tail -f /var/www/attendance/storage/logs/laravel.log
```

### Database connection error
```bash
# Test connection
sudo mysql -u attendance_user -p
# Enter password from .env

# Check database exists
SHOW DATABASES;

# Select database
USE attendance_db;

# Show tables
SHOW TABLES;
```

### Permission errors
```bash
# Fix ownership
sudo chown -R www-data:www-data /var/www/attendance

# Fix permissions
sudo chmod 755 /var/www/attendance
sudo chmod 775 /var/www/attendance/storage /var/www/attendance/bootstrap/cache
```

## Support

For issues, check:
1. [DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md](DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md) - Detailed Arabic guide
2. [QUICK_DEPLOY.md](QUICK_DEPLOY.md) - Quick reference
3. Application logs in `/var/www/attendance/storage/logs/`
4. Nginx logs in `/var/log/nginx/`
5. System logs: `sudo journalctl -xe`

**Last Updated:** March 2026
**Tested on:** Ubuntu 24.04 LTS, Hostinger VPS KVM 2

### 14. `artisan`

```
#!/usr/bin/env php
<?php

define('LARAVEL_START', microtime(true));

/*
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| Register The Auto Loader
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
|
| Composer provides a convenient, automatically generated class loader
| for our application. We just need to utilize it! We'll require it
| into the script here so that we do not have to worry about the
| loading of any of our classes manually. It's great to relax.
|
*/

require __DIR__.'/vendor/autoload.php';

$app = require_once __DIR__.'/bootstrap/app.php';

/*
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| Run The Artisan Application
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
|
| When we run the console application, the current CLI command will be
| executed in this console and the response sent back to a terminal
| or another output device for the developers. Here goes nothing!
|
*/

$kernel = $app->make(Illuminate\Contracts\Console\Kernel::class);

$status = $kernel->handle(
    $input = new Symfony\Component\Console\Input\ArgvInput,
    new Symfony\Component\Console\Output\ConsoleOutput
);

/*
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
| Shutdown The Application
|--------------------------------------------------------------------------
|
| Once Artisan has finished running, we will fire off the shutdown events
| so that any final work may be done by the application before we shut
| down the process. This is the last thing to happen to the request.
|
*/

$kernel->terminate($input, $status);

exit($status);
```

---

### 15. `backup.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# Backup Script for Attendance Application
# Schedule with cron: 0 2 * * * /var/www/attendance/backup.sh

set -e

APP_DIR="/var/www/attendance"
BACKUP_DIR="/var/backups/attendance"
DATE=$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S)
HOSTNAME=$(hostname)

# Create backup directory if not exists
mkdir -p $BACKUP_DIR

echo "[$(date)] Starting backup..."

# Backup database
echo "Backing up database..."
mysqldump -u attendance_user -pSecurePassword123! attendance_db | gzip > $BACKUP_DIR/database_$DATE.sql.gz

# Backup application files
echo "Backing up application files..."
tar -czf $BACKUP_DIR/app_files_$DATE.tar.gz \
    --exclude='storage/logs' \
    --exclude='node_modules' \
    --exclude='.git' \
    --exclude='vendor' \
    -C /var/www attendance

# Keep only last 30 days of backups
find $BACKUP_DIR -type f -mtime +30 -delete

echo "[$(date)] Backup completed successfully!"
echo "Database backup: $BACKUP_DIR/database_$DATE.sql.gz"
echo "Files backup: $BACKUP_DIR/app_files_$DATE.tar.gz"

# Optional: Send to remote storage
# aws s3 cp $BACKUP_DIR s3://your-bucket/backups/ --recursive
```

---

### 16. `bind_domain.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Bind the live Laravel app to mycorner.site and issue SSL."""

import paramiko
import sys
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
DOMAIN = "mycorner.site"
WWW_DOMAIN = "www.mycorner.site"
APP_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

NGINX_HTTP = f"""server {{
    listen 80;
    listen [::]:80;
    server_name {DOMAIN} {WWW_DOMAIN};

    root {APP_PATH}/public;
    index index.php index.html;

    access_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_access.log;
    error_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log;

    client_max_body_size 100M;

    add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN always;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff always;
    server_tokens off;

    location / {{
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.php?$query_string;
    }}

    location ~ \.php$ {{
        fastcgi_split_path_info ^(.+\.php)(/.+)$;
        fastcgi_pass unix:/run/php/php8.3-fpm.sock;
        fastcgi_index index.php;
        include fastcgi_params;
        fastcgi_param SCRIPT_FILENAME $document_root$fastcgi_script_name;
        fastcgi_param PATH_INFO $fastcgi_path_info;
    }}

    location ~ /\.ht {{
        deny all;
    }}

    location ~* \.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|ico|css|js|svg|woff|woff2|ttf|eot)$ {{
        expires 365d;
        add_header Cache-Control \"public\";
    }}
}}
"""


def run(ssh, command, timeout=120, show=True):
    stdin, stdout, stderr = ssh.exec_command(command, timeout=timeout)
    stdout.channel.settimeout(timeout)
    output = stdout.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
    error = stderr.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
    if show:
        if output:
            print(output[:2000])
        if error and "warning" not in error.lower() and "notice" not in error.lower():
            print("ERR:", error[:1000])
    return stdout.channel.recv_exit_status(), output, error


def main():
    print("[*] Connecting to VPS...")
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)
    print("[+] Connected")

    print("\n[1] Backing up current config...")
    run(ssh, f"cp /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance.bak.$(date +%s) 2>/dev/null || true", show=False)
    run(ssh, f"cp {APP_PATH}/.env {APP_PATH}/.env.bak.$(date +%s)", show=False)
    print("[+] Backups created")

    print("\n[2] Writing domain-aware Nginx config...")
    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
    with sftp.file("/etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance", "w") as remote_file:
        remote_file.write(NGINX_HTTP)
    sftp.close()
    run(ssh, "ln -sf /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/attendance", show=False)
    code, out, err = run(ssh, "nginx -t 2>&1")
    if code != 0:
        print("[!] Nginx config test failed")
        ssh.close()
        sys.exit(1)
    run(ssh, "systemctl reload nginx")
    print("[+] Nginx updated")

    print("\n[3] Updating Laravel environment...")
    env_updates = [
        f"sed -i 's|^APP_URL=.*|APP_URL=https://{DOMAIN}|' {APP_PATH}/.env",
        f"grep -q '^SESSION_DOMAIN=' {APP_PATH}/.env && sed -i 's|^SESSION_DOMAIN=.*|SESSION_DOMAIN=.{DOMAIN}|' {APP_PATH}/.env || echo 'SESSION_DOMAIN=.{DOMAIN}' >> {APP_PATH}/.env",
        f"grep -q '^SANCTUM_STATEFUL_DOMAINS=' {APP_PATH}/.env && sed -i 's|^SANCTUM_STATEFUL_DOMAINS=.*|SANCTUM_STATEFUL_DOMAINS={DOMAIN},{WWW_DOMAIN}|' {APP_PATH}/.env || echo 'SANCTUM_STATEFUL_DOMAINS={DOMAIN},{WWW_DOMAIN}' >> {APP_PATH}/.env",
    ]
    for command in env_updates:
        run(ssh, command, show=False)
    run(ssh, f"grep -E '^(APP_URL|SESSION_DOMAIN|SANCTUM_STATEFUL_DOMAINS)=' {APP_PATH}/.env")
    run(ssh, f"cd {APP_PATH} && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1", timeout=180)
    run(ssh, f"cd {APP_PATH} && php artisan config:cache 2>&1", timeout=180)
    run(ssh, f"cd {APP_PATH} && php artisan route:cache 2>&1", timeout=180)
    print("[+] Laravel env updated")

    print("\n[4] Issuing Let's Encrypt certificate...")
    certbot_cmd = f"certbot --nginx -d {DOMAIN} -d {WWW_DOMAIN} --non-interactive --agree-tos --register-unsafely-without-email --redirect"
    code, out, err = run(ssh, certbot_cmd, timeout=600)
    if code != 0:
        print("[!] Certbot did not complete successfully")
        print(out[:1500])
        print(err[:1500])
        ssh.close()
        sys.exit(2)
    print("[+] SSL issued and redirect enabled")

    print("\n[5] Final verification...")
    run(ssh, "nginx -t 2>&1")
    run(ssh, "systemctl is-active nginx")
    run(ssh, "systemctl is-active php8.3-fpm")
    run(ssh, f"curl -I https://{DOMAIN}/admin/login 2>/dev/null | head -5")
    run(ssh, f"curl -I https://{WWW_DOMAIN}/admin/login 2>/dev/null | head -5")

    print("\n[+] Domain binding complete")
    print(f"Site: https://{DOMAIN}")
    print(f"Admin: https://{DOMAIN}/admin/login")
    print(f"WWW: https://{WWW_DOMAIN}/admin/login")

    ssh.close()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Check dashboard 500 error"""
import paramiko

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, t=30):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(t)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        if out: print(out[:1500])
        if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower():
            print("ERR:", err[:500])
        return out

    print("=== Laravel Error Log (last 50 lines) ===")
    r("tail -60 %s/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n=== Nginx Error Log ===")
    r("tail -20 /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log 2>/dev/null || tail -20 /var/log/nginx/error.log 2>/dev/null")

    print("\n=== Test dashboard route directly ===")
    r("curl -v http://localhost/admin/dashboard 2>&1 | tail -30")

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

### 20. `debug_api.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Test /api/realtime-dashboard endpoint with proper login session"""
import paramiko
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, t=30):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(t)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        if out: print(out[:2000])
        if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower():
            print("ERR:", err[:500])
        return out

    # Enable debug mode to see error
    r("sed -i 's/APP_DEBUG=false/APP_DEBUG=true/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:clear 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Step 1: Get login page and CSRF
    print("[1] Get CSRF token...")
    r("curl -s -c /tmp/test_cookies.txt http://localhost/admin/login -o /tmp/login_page.html")
    csrf = r("grep -oP '(?<=name=\"_token\" value=\")[^\"]+' /tmp/login_page.html | head -1")
    print("CSRF:", csrf[:20] if csrf else "NOT FOUND")

    if not csrf:
        print("No CSRF - trying different approach")
        csrf = r("grep -oP '\"csrfToken\":\"\\K[^\"]+' /tmp/login_page.html | head -1")

    # Step 2: GET XSRF cookie
    r("cat /tmp/test_cookies.txt")

    # Step 3: Login with proper XSRF token
    print("\n[2] Login...")
    xsrf = r("grep 'XSRF' /tmp/test_cookies.txt | awk '{print $NF}' | python3 -c \"import sys, urllib.parse; print(urllib.parse.unquote(sys.stdin.read().strip()))\" 2>/dev/null | head -1")
    print("XSRF:", xsrf[:30] if xsrf else "NOT FOUND")

    r("""curl -s \\
        -b /tmp/test_cookies.txt \\
        -c /tmp/test_cookies.txt \\
        -H 'X-XSRF-TOKEN: %s' \\
        -X POST http://localhost/admin/login \\
        -d '_token=%s&username=admin&password=Admin@123456' \\
        -D /tmp/login_headers.txt \\
        -o /tmp/login_resp.html \\
        -w 'Login: %%{http_code}'""" % (xsrf, csrf))

    r("head -3 /tmp/login_headers.txt")

    # Step 4: Test the API endpoint WITH session cookies
    print("\n[3] Test /api/realtime-dashboard with session...")
    r("""curl -s \\
        -b /tmp/test_cookies.txt \\
        -H 'Accept: application/json' \\
        http://localhost/api/realtime-dashboard \\
        -w '\\nHTTP: %%{http_code}'""")

    # Step 5: Check fresh log
    print("\n[4] Fresh Laravel log...")
    r("tail -30 %s/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null | grep -v '^#\\|^Stack'" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Step 6: Test API directly via PHP
    print("\n[5] Direct test via artisan tinker...")
    r("""cd %s && php artisan tinker --execute="
try {
    \$branches = App\\\\Models\\\\Branch::active()->withCount('employees')->get();
    echo 'Branches with count: OK, count=' . \$branches->count() . PHP_EOL;
} catch (\\\\Exception \$e) {
    echo 'ERROR: ' . \$e->getMessage() . PHP_EOL;
    echo 'at ' . \$e->getFile() . ':' . \$e->getLine() . PHP_EOL;
}
" 2>&1""" % REMOTE_PATH, t=20)

    # Disable debug  
    r("sed -i 's/APP_DEBUG=true/APP_DEBUG=false/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Get the actual 500 error by testing dashboard after proper login"""
import paramiko
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, t=30):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(t)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        if out: print(out[:2000])
        if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower():
            print("ERR:", err[:500])
        return out

    # Clear the log first
    r("truncate -s 0 %s/storage/logs/laravel.log" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Use artisan tinker to test the DashboardController logic
    print("[1] Test DashboardController logic via artisan tinker...")
    r("""cd %s && php artisan tinker --execute="
try {
    \$stats = App\\\\Models\\\\Attendance::getTodayStats();
    echo 'Stats OK: ' . json_encode(\$stats) . PHP_EOL;
    \$branchCount = App\\\\Models\\\\Branch::active()->count();
    echo 'Branches OK: ' . \$branchCount . PHP_EOL;
    \$empCount = App\\\\Models\\\\Employee::active()->count();
    echo 'Employees OK: ' . \$empCount . PHP_EOL;
} catch (\\\\Exception \$e) {
    echo 'ERROR: ' . \$e->getMessage() . PHP_EOL;
    echo 'FILE: ' . \$e->getFile() . ':' . \$e->getLine() . PHP_EOL;
}
" 2>&1""" % REMOTE_PATH, t=30)

    # Check if Employee has 'active' scope
    print("\n[2] Check Employee model scopes...")
    r("grep -n 'scopeActive\\|deleted_at\\|softDelete' %s/app/Models/Employee.php 2>/dev/null | head -10" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Check Branch model 'active' scope
    print("\n[3] Check Branch model scopes...")
    r("grep -n 'scopeActive\\|active' %s/app/Models/Branch.php 2>/dev/null | head -10" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Check view files exist on server
    print("\n[4] Check view components on server...")
    r("ls %s/resources/views/components/ 2>/dev/null" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("ls %s/resources/views/layouts/ 2>/dev/null" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("ls %s/resources/views/admin/ 2>/dev/null | head -20" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Check public assets
    print("\n[5] Check public assets...")
    r("ls %s/public/assets/fonts/ 2>/dev/null" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("ls %s/public/ 2>/dev/null" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Now enable debug mode temporarily and check
    print("\n[6] Check Laravel log after tinker test...")
    r("cat %s/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null | head -50" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Test real page with debug enabled
    print("\n[7] Enable debug briefly and test dashboard...")
    r("sed -i 's/APP_DEBUG=false/APP_DEBUG=true/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    # Simulate request using PHP CLI to render dashboard
    r("""cd %s && php -r "
\\$_SERVER['HTTP_HOST'] = 'localhost';
\\$_SERVER['REQUEST_URI'] = '/admin/dashboard';
\\$base = '%s';
require \\$base.'/vendor/autoload.php';
\\$app = require \\$base.'/bootstrap/app.php';
\\$kernel = \\$app->make(Illuminate\\Contracts\\Http\\Kernel::class);
\\$request = Illuminate\\Http\\Request::create('/admin/dashboard', 'GET');
try {
    \\$response = \\$kernel->handle(\\$request);
    echo 'HTTP: ' . \\$response->getStatusCode() . PHP_EOL;
    if (\\$response->getStatusCode() == 500) {
        echo substr(\\$response->getContent(), 0, 2000);
    }
} catch (Exception \\$e) {
    echo 'Exception: ' . \\$e->getMessage() . PHP_EOL;
    echo 'at ' . \\$e->getFile() . ':' . \\$e->getLine();
}
" 2>&1 | head -50""" % (REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH), t=30)

    # Revert debug
    r("sed -i 's/APP_DEBUG=true/APP_DEBUG=false/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 22. `debug_dashboard.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Deep debug: login then hit dashboard, get fresh errors"""
import paramiko
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, t=30):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(t)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        if out: print(out[:2000])
        if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower():
            print("ERR:", err[:500])
        return out

    # 1. Clear old log and test fresh
    print("[1] Clearing Laravel log then hitting dashboard...")
    r("echo '' > %s/storage/logs/laravel.log" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Test dashboard with a session cookie (simulate login)
    # First get login page to get CSRF
    r("curl -s -c /tmp/cookies.txt http://localhost/admin/login -o /dev/null -w 'Login page: %{http_code}'")

    # Get CSRF token
    csrf, _ = r("curl -s http://localhost/admin/login | grep '_token' | head -1"), None
    csrf = r("curl -s http://localhost/admin/login | grep -oP 'name=\"_token\" value=\"\\K[^\"]+' | head -1")

    print("\nCSRF token:", csrf[:20] if csrf else "NOT FOUND")

    # Post login
    if csrf:
        print("\n[2] Posting login...")
        r("""curl -s -b /tmp/cookies.txt -c /tmp/cookies.txt \\
            -X POST http://localhost/admin/login \\
            -d "_token=%s&username=admin&password=Admin@123456" \\
            -L -w 'Login POST: %%{http_code}' -o /tmp/login_response.html""" % csrf)

        r("head -5 /tmp/login_response.html 2>/dev/null")

        print("\n[3] Hitting dashboard with session...")
        r("""curl -s -b /tmp/cookies.txt \\
            http://localhost/admin/dashboard \\
            -w 'Dashboard: %%{http_code}' -o /tmp/dash_response.html""")

        # Check response
        r("head -20 /tmp/dash_response.html 2>/dev/null | grep -i 'error\\|exception\\|500' || echo 'no error in HTML head'")

    print("\n[4] Fresh Laravel log after request...")
    time.sleep(1)
    r("cat %s/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null | grep -v '^#\\|Stack trace' | head -40" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[5] Check DashboardController...")
    r("cat %s/app/Http/Controllers/Admin/DashboardController.php 2>/dev/null" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[6] Check what files are missing from public/assets/...")
    r("ls -la %s/public/assets/ 2>/dev/null | head -20" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("ls -la %s/public/assets/fonts/tajawal/ 2>/dev/null || echo 'tajawal dir missing'")

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 23. `deploy.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# Laravel Attendance Application Deployment Script
# For Ubuntu 24.04 LTS on Hostinger VPS

set -e  # Exit on error

echo "========================================"
echo "Laravel Attendance App - Deployment"
echo "========================================"

# Colors for output
RED='\033[0;31m'
GREEN='\033[0;32m'
YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
NC='\033[0m' # No Color

# Configuration variables
APP_DIR="/var/www/attendance"
APP_USER="www-data"
DOMAIN="your-domain.com"  # Change this
DB_NAME="attendance_db"
DB_USER="attendance_user"

# Step 1: Update system
echo -e "${YELLOW}[1/12] Updating system packages...${NC}"
sudo apt-get update
sudo apt-get upgrade -y

# Step 2: Install required packages
echo -e "${YELLOW}[2/12] Installing PHP and dependencies...${NC}"
sudo apt-get install -y \
    software-properties-common \
    curl \
    wget \
    git \
    zip \
    unzip \
    nginx \
    mysql-server \
    redis-server \
    certbot \
    python3-certbot-nginx

# Step 3: Install PHP 8.2 with required extensions
echo -e "${YELLOW}[3/12] Installing PHP 8.2...${NC}"
sudo add-apt-repository ppa:ondrej/php -y
sudo apt-get update
sudo apt-get install -y \
    php8.2 \
    php8.2-fpm \
    php8.2-mysql \
    php8.2-mbstring \
    php8.2-xml \
    php8.2-bcmath \
    php8.2-json \
    php8.2-curl \
    php8.2-gd \
    php8.2-zip \
    php8.2-intl \
    php8.2-redis

# Step 4: Enable PHP-FPM
echo -e "${YELLOW}[4/12] Enabling PHP-FPM...${NC}"
sudo systemctl start php8.2-fpm
sudo systemctl enable php8.2-fpm

# Step 5: Install Composer
echo -e "${YELLOW}[5/12] Installing Composer...${NC}"
curl -sS https://getcomposer.org/installer | sudo php -- --install-dir=/usr/local/bin --filename=composer

# Step 6: Install Node.js and npm
echo -e "${YELLOW}[6/12] Installing Node.js and npm...${NC}"
curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_20.x | sudo -E bash -
sudo apt-get install -y nodejs

# Step 7: Create application directory
echo -e "${YELLOW}[7/12] Creating application directory...${NC}"
sudo mkdir -p $APP_DIR
sudo chown -R $APP_USER:$APP_USER $APP_DIR

# Step 8: Clone or upload application
echo -e "${YELLOW}[8/12] Setting up application files...${NC}"
# If using git clone:
# sudo -u $APP_USER git clone https://your-repo-url.git $APP_DIR
# For now, assume files are already uploaded via SFTP

# Step 9: Install PHP dependencies
echo -e "${YELLOW}[9/12] Installing PHP dependencies...${NC}"
cd $APP_DIR
sudo -u $APP_USER composer install --optimize-autoloader --no-dev

# Step 10: Install Node dependencies and build assets
echo -e "${YELLOW}[10/12] Building frontend assets...${NC}"
sudo -u $APP_USER npm install
sudo -u $APP_USER npm run build

# Step 11: Generate app key and setup environment
echo -e "${YELLOW}[11/12] Configuring application...${NC}"
sudo -u $APP_USER cp .env.example .env 2>/dev/null || true
sudo -u $APP_USER php artisan key:generate --force
sudo -u $APP_USER chmod 775 storage bootstrap/cache
sudo -u $APP_USER php artisan migrate --force
sudo -u $APP_USER php artisan optimize

# Step 12: Configure Nginx
echo -e "${YELLOW}[12/12] Configuring Nginx...${NC}"
# Nginx config will be created separately. See nginx.conf file.

# Final messages
echo ""
echo -e "${GREEN}========================================"
echo "Deployment completed!"
echo "========================================${NC}"
echo ""
echo "Next steps:"
echo "1. Upload nginx.conf to: /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance"
echo "2. Enable site: sudo ln -s /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/"
echo "3. Test nginx: sudo nginx -t"
echo "4. Restart nginx: sudo systemctl restart nginx"
echo "5. Setup SSL: sudo certbot --nginx -d your-domain.com"
echo "6. Configure MySQL database in .env file"
echo "7. Test application at: http://your-domain.com"
echo ""
```

---

### 24. `deploy_automated.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Secure SSH Deployment Script for Attendance Application
"""

import paramiko
import sys
import time
import os

class SSHDeployment:
    def __init__(self, host, username, password, port=22):
        self.host = host
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
        self.port = port
        self.ssh = None
        self.sftp = None
    
    def connect(self):
        """Connect to SSH server"""
        try:
            msg = "[*] Connecting to %s@%s..." % (self.username, self.host)
            print(msg)
            self.ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
            self.ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
            self.ssh.connect(
                self.host,
                port=self.port,
                username=self.username,
                password=self.password,
                timeout=30
            )
            print("[+] Connected successfully!\n")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            print("[!] Connection failed: %s" % str(e))
            return False
    
    def execute_command(self, command, show_output=True):
        """Execute command on remote server"""
        try:
            stdin, stdout, stderr = self.ssh.exec_command(command)
            stdout.channel.settimeout(300)
            
            output = stdout.read().decode('utf-8', errors='ignore')
            error = stderr.read().decode('utf-8', errors='ignore')
            
            if show_output and output:
                print(output)
            if error and show_output:
                print("[!] %s" % error)
            
            return stdout.channel.recv_exit_status() == 0, output, error
        except Exception as e:
            print("[!] Command execution failed: %s" % str(e))
            return False, "", str(e)
    
    def deploy(self):
        """Run the complete deployment"""
        if not self.connect():
            return False
        
        print("\n" + "="*50)
        print("DEPLOYMENT PROCESS")
        print("="*50 + "\n")
        
        print("[1] Updating system packages...")
        self.execute_command("sudo apt-get update && sudo apt-get upgrade -y")
        
        print("\n[2] Installing required packages...")
        self.execute_command("sudo apt-get install -y software-properties-common curl git zip unzip nginx mysql-server redis-server certbot python3-certbot-nginx supervisor")
        
        print("\n[3] Installing PHP 8.2...")
        self.execute_command("sudo add-apt-repository ppa:ondrej/php -y")
        self.execute_command("sudo apt-get update")
        self.execute_command("sudo apt-get install -y php8.2 php8.2-fpm php8.2-mysql php8.2-mbstring php8.2-xml php8.2-bcmath php8.2-json php8.2-curl php8.2-gd php8.2-zip php8.2-intl php8.2-redis")
        
        print("\n[4] Enabling services...")
        self.execute_command("sudo systemctl start php8.2-fpm && sudo systemctl enable php8.2-fpm")
        self.execute_command("sudo systemctl start nginx && sudo systemctl enable nginx")
        self.execute_command("sudo systemctl start mysql && sudo systemctl enable mysql")
        self.execute_command("sudo systemctl start redis-server && sudo systemctl enable redis-server")
        
        print("\n[5] Installing Composer...")
        self.execute_command("curl -sS https://getcomposer.org/installer | sudo php -- --install-dir=/usr/local/bin --filename=composer")
        
        print("\n[6] Installing Node.js...")
        self.execute_command("curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_20.x | sudo -E bash -")
        self.execute_command("sudo apt-get install -y nodejs")
        
        print("\n[7] Setting up application directory...")
        self.execute_command("sudo mkdir -p /var/www/attendance")
        self.execute_command("sudo chown -R www-data:www-data /var/www/attendance")
        
        print("\n[8] Setting up MySQL database...")
        db_commands = [
            "sudo mysql -e 'CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS attendance_db CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;'",
            "sudo mysql -e \"CREATE USER IF NOT EXISTS 'attendance_user'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED BY 'Goolbx512@@@@';\"",
            "sudo mysql -e 'GRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON attendance_db.* TO attendance_user@localhost;'",
            "sudo mysql -e 'FLUSH PRIVILEGES;'"
        ]
        for cmd in db_commands:
            self.execute_command(cmd)
        
        print("\n[9] Verifying services...")
        self.execute_command("sudo systemctl status nginx --no-pager")
        
        print("\n[+] Server preparation completed!")
        print("\n[*] Next steps:")
        print("1. Upload your application files to /var/www/attendance")
        print("2. Configure .env file with database credentials")
        print("3. Run: php artisan migrate")
        print("4. Configure Nginx with the provided nginx.conf")
        
        self.disconnect()
        return True
    
    def disconnect(self):
        """Close SSH connection"""
        if self.sftp:
            try:
                self.sftp.close()
            except:
                pass
        if self.ssh:
            try:
                self.ssh.close()
            except:
                pass
            print("\n[+] Disconnected from server")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    HOST = "187.77.173.160"
    USERNAME = "root"
    PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
    
    deployment = SSHDeployment(HOST, USERNAME, PASSWORD)
    success = deployment.deploy()
    
    sys.exit(0 if success else 1)
```

### 25. `deploy_fixes.py`

```python
import paramiko
import os
import sys

HOST = '187.77.173.160'
USER = 'root'
PASS = 'Goolbx512@@@@'
REMOTE_BASE = '/var/www/attendance'

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USER, password=PASS, timeout=15)
    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()

    local_base = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))

    files_to_upload = [
        # Critical fixes
        ('resources/views/layouts/admin.blade.php', 'resources/views/layouts/admin.blade.php'),
        ('resources/views/admin/login.blade.php', 'resources/views/admin/login.blade.php'),
        ('app/Services/TwoFactorService.php', 'app/Services/TwoFactorService.php'),
        # High fixes
        ('app/Http/Controllers/Admin/BranchController.php', 'app/Http/Controllers/Admin/BranchController.php'),
        ('app/Services/BackupService.php', 'app/Services/BackupService.php'),
        ('routes/api.php', 'routes/api.php'),
        # Medium fixes
        ('routes/web.php', 'routes/web.php'),
        ('config/cors.php', 'config/cors.php'),
        # Fonts CSS
        ('public/assets/fonts/tajawal.css', 'public/assets/fonts/tajawal.css'),
    ]

    # Upload font files
    font_dir = os.path.join(local_base, 'public', 'assets', 'fonts', 'tajawal')
    if os.path.isdir(font_dir):
        for fname in os.listdir(font_dir):
            if fname.endswith('.woff2'):
                files_to_upload.append(
                    (f'public/assets/fonts/tajawal/{fname}', f'public/assets/fonts/tajawal/{fname}')
                )

    # Create remote font directory
    remote_dirs = [
        f'{REMOTE_BASE}/public/assets/fonts/tajawal',
        f'{REMOTE_BASE}/resources/views/layouts',
        f'{REMOTE_BASE}/resources/views/admin',
        f'{REMOTE_BASE}/app/Services',
        f'{REMOTE_BASE}/app/Http/Controllers/Admin',
    ]
    for d in remote_dirs:
        try:
            sftp.mkdir(d)
        except IOError:
            pass  # already exists

    print(f"Uploading {len(files_to_upload)} files...")
    for local_rel, remote_rel in files_to_upload:
        local_path = os.path.join(local_base, local_rel.replace('/', os.sep))
        remote_path = f'{REMOTE_BASE}/{remote_rel}'
        if not os.path.exists(local_path):
            print(f"  SKIP (not found): {local_rel}")
            continue
        sftp.put(local_path, remote_path)
        print(f"  OK: {remote_rel}")

    # Fix permissions and clear cache
    commands = [
        f'chown -R www-data:www-data {REMOTE_BASE}/resources {REMOTE_BASE}/app {REMOTE_BASE}/routes {REMOTE_BASE}/config {REMOTE_BASE}/public/assets/fonts/tajawal',
        f'cd {REMOTE_BASE} && php artisan config:clear',
        f'cd {REMOTE_BASE} && php artisan route:clear',
        f'cd {REMOTE_BASE} && php artisan view:clear',
        f'cd {REMOTE_BASE} && php artisan cache:clear',
    ]

    print("\nRunning server commands...")
    for cmd in commands:
        stdin, stdout, stderr = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        out = stdout.read().decode().strip()
        err = stderr.read().decode().strip()
        if out:
            print(f"  {out}")
        if err and 'Warning' not in err:
            print(f"  ERR: {err}")

    # Verify dashboard
    print("\nVerifying...")
    stdin, stdout, stderr = ssh.exec_command('curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" https://mycorner.site/admin/login')
    code = stdout.read().decode().strip()
    print(f"  Login page: HTTP {code}")

    stdin, stdout, stderr = ssh.exec_command(f'ls -la {REMOTE_BASE}/public/assets/fonts/tajawal/ | head -5')
    out = stdout.read().decode().strip()
    print(f"  Fonts: {out}")

    # Delete Python scripts and credential files from server if they exist
    print("\nCleaning credential files from server...")
    stdin, stdout, stderr = ssh.exec_command(f'find {REMOTE_BASE} -maxdepth 1 -name "*.py" -delete 2>&1; echo "Python scripts cleaned"')
    print(f"  {stdout.read().decode().strip()}")
    for f in ['DEPLOYMENT_COMPLETE.md', 'DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md', 'FINAL_STEPS_AR.md']:
        ssh.exec_command(f'rm -f {REMOTE_BASE}/{f}')
    print("  Credential files cleaned")

    sftp.close()
    ssh.close()
    print("\nDone! All fixes deployed.")

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

### 26. `deploy_route_fix.py`

```python
import io
import paramiko

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
APP_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"
LOCAL_FILE = r"c:\Users\IT\Desktop\online_4-main\attendance-laravel\routes\web.php"

ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
with open(LOCAL_FILE, "rb") as f:
    sftp.putfo(f, APP_PATH + "/routes/web.php")
sftp.close()

def run(cmd, timeout=120):
    i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd, timeout=timeout)
    o.channel.settimeout(timeout)
    out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
    err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
    if out:
        print(out[:1500])
    if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "notice" not in err.lower():
        print("ERR:", err[:600])

run(f"cd {APP_PATH} && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1", 180)
run(f"cd {APP_PATH} && php artisan route:cache 2>&1", 180)
run(f"cd {APP_PATH} && php artisan config:cache 2>&1", 180)
ssh.close()
```

---

### 27. `deploy_v2.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Smart SSH Deployment Script for Attendance Application
Waits for previous apt-get operations to complete
"""

import paramiko
import sys
import time
import os

class SSHDeployment:
    def __init__(self, host, username, password, port=22):
        self.host = host
        self.username = username
        self.password = password
        self.port = port
        self.ssh = None
    
    def connect(self):
        """Connect to SSH server"""
        try:
            msg = "[*] Connecting to %s@%s..." % (self.username, self.host)
            print(msg)
            self.ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
            self.ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
            self.ssh.connect(
                self.host,
                port=self.port,
                username=self.username,
                password=self.password,
                timeout=30
            )
            print("[+] Connected successfully!\n")
            return True
        except Exception as e:
            print("[!] Connection failed: %s" % str(e))
            return False
    
    def wait_for_lock(self, max_wait=600):
        """Wait for dpkg lock to be released"""
        print("[*] Waiting for package manager to be available...")
        waited = 0
        while waited < max_wait:
            stdin, stdout, stderr = self.ssh.exec_command("lsof /var/lib/dpkg/lock-frontend 2>/dev/null | wc -l")
            result = stdout.read().decode('utf-8', errors='ignore').strip()
            if result == "0":
                print("[+] Package manager is ready!")
                return True
            print("[.] Still waiting... (%d seconds)" % waited)
            time.sleep(30)
            waited += 30
        
        print("[!] Timeout waiting for package manager")
        return False
    
    def execute_command(self, command, show_output=True):
        """Execute command on remote server"""
        try:
            stdin, stdout, stderr = self.ssh.exec_command(command)
            stdout.channel.settimeout(600)
            
            output = stdout.read().decode('utf-8', errors='ignore')
            error = stderr.read().decode('utf-8', errors='ignore')
            
            if show_output and output:
                print(output[:1000])
            if error and show_output:
                print("[!] %s" % error[:500])
            
            return stdout.channel.recv_exit_status() == 0, output, error
        except Exception as e:
            print("[!] Command execution failed: %s" % str(e))
            return False, "", str(e)
    
    def deploy(self):
        """Run the complete deployment"""
        if not self.connect():
            return False
        
        if not self.wait_for_lock():
            print("[!] Cannot proceed - package manager is locked")
            return False
        
        print("\n" + "="*50)
        print("DEPLOYMENT PROCESS")
        print("="*50 + "\n")
        
        print("[1] Updating system packages...")
        self.execute_command("sudo apt-get update")
        
        print("\n[2] Installing required packages...")
        packages = "software-properties-common curl git zip unzip nginx mysql-server redis-server certbot python3-certbot-nginx supervisor"
        self.execute_command("sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive apt-get install -y %s" % packages)
        
        print("\n[3] Installing PHP 8.2...")
        self.execute_command("sudo add-apt-repository ppa:ondrej/php -y")
        self.execute_command("sudo apt-get update")
        php_packages = "php8.2 php8.2-fpm php8.2-mysql php8.2-mbstring php8.2-xml php8.2-bcmath php8.2-json php8.2-curl php8.2-gd php8.2-zip php8.2-intl php8.2-redis"
        self.execute_command("sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive apt-get install -y %s" % php_packages)
        
        print("\n[4] Enabling and starting services...")
        services = ["php8.2-fpm", "nginx", "mysql", "redis-server"]
        for service in services:
            self.execute_command("sudo systemctl start %s" % service)
            self.execute_command("sudo systemctl enable %s" % service)
        
        print("\n[5] Installing Composer...")
        self.execute_command("curl -sS https://getcomposer.org/installer | sudo php -- --install-dir=/usr/local/bin --filename=composer", show_output=False)
        
        print("[6] Installing Node.js...")
        self.execute_command("curl -fsSL https://deb.nodesource.com/setup_20.x | sudo -E bash -", show_output=False)
        self.execute_command("sudo DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive apt-get install -y nodejs", show_output=False)
        
        print("\n[7] Creating application directory...")
        self.execute_command("sudo mkdir -p /var/www/attendance")
        self.execute_command("sudo chown -R www-data:www-data /var/www/attendance")
        
        print("\n[8] Setting up MySQL database...")
        self.execute_command("sudo mysql -e 'CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS attendance_db CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;'", show_output=False)
        self.execute_command("sudo mysql -e \"CREATE USER IF NOT EXISTS 'attendance_user'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED BY 'Goolbx512@@@@';\"", show_output=False)
        self.execute_command("sudo mysql -e 'GRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON attendance_db.* TO attendance_user@localhost;'", show_output=False)
        self.execute_command("sudo mysql -e 'FLUSH PRIVILEGES;'", show_output=False)
        
        print("\n[+] SUCCESS! Server preparation completed!")
        print("\n[*] Next steps:")
        print("   1. Copy your application files to /var/www/attendance")
        print("   2. Copy nginx.conf to /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance")
        print("   3. Enable Nginx site and install SSL")
        print("   4. Update .env with database credentials")
        print("   5. Run: php artisan migrate")
        
        self.disconnect()
        return True
    
    def disconnect(self):
        """Close SSH connection"""
        if self.ssh:
            try:
                self.ssh.close()
            except:
                pass

if __name__ == "__main__":
    HOST = "187.77.173.160"
    USERNAME = "root" 
    PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
    
    deployment = SSHDeployment(HOST, USERNAME, PASSWORD)
    success = deployment.deploy()
    
    print("\n[*] Deployment script finished.")
    sys.exit(0 if success else 1)
```

### 29. `diagnose.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Diagnose and fix remaining issues"""
import paramiko

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, timeout=90, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(timeout)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out: print(out[:1000])
            if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower() and "notice" not in err.lower():
                print("ERR:", err[:500])
        return out, err

    # 1. Check available routes
    print("[1] Checking registered routes (web)...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:list --path=login 2>&1 | head -20" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:list 2>&1 | grep -i 'GET.*/' | head -30" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # 2. Fix Redis
    print("\n[2] Fixing Redis...")
    r("systemctl start redis-server")
    r("systemctl enable redis-server")
    out, _ = r("systemctl is-active redis-server")
    print("Redis:", out)

    # 3. Check seeders and admin table
    print("\n[3] Checking DB tables...")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SHOW TABLES;' 2>/dev/null")

    print("\n[4] Checking admins table structure...")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'DESCRIBE admins;' 2>/dev/null")

    print("\n[5] Checking users table...")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SELECT id,name,email,role FROM users LIMIT 5;' 2>/dev/null || echo 'no users table'")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SELECT COUNT(*) FROM admins;' 2>/dev/null")

    print("\n[6] Running seeders again...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan db:seed --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[7] Check admin records after seeding...")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SELECT id,name,email FROM admins;' 2>/dev/null")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SELECT id,name,email,role FROM users LIMIT 5;' 2>/dev/null || echo 'N/A'")

    print("\n[8] Check Laravel log for seeder errors...")
    r("tail -30 %s/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null | grep -i 'error\\|exception' | tail -10" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # 9. Test actual routing
    print("\n[9] Testing main page redirect location...")
    r("curl -s -D - -o /dev/null http://localhost/ | grep -i 'location:\\|http'")

    print("\n[10] Test all important routes...")
    routes_to_test = ["/", "/login", "/admin", "/admin/login", "/api/", "/api/v1/", "/dashboard"]
    for route in routes_to_test:
        out, _ = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w '%s -> %%{http_code}' http://localhost%s" % (route, route), show=False)
        print(out)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 30. `download_fonts.py`

```python
import urllib.request
import re
import os

base_dir = os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), 'public', 'assets', 'fonts', 'tajawal')
os.makedirs(base_dir, exist_ok=True)

ua = 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36'
weights = [300, 400, 500, 700, 800]

for w in weights:
    url = f'https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Tajawal:wght@{w}&display=swap'
    req = urllib.request.Request(url, headers={'User-Agent': ua})
    css = urllib.request.urlopen(req).read().decode()
    blocks = css.split('@font-face')
    for block in blocks:
        if not block.strip():
            continue
        url_match = re.search(r'url\((https://[^)]+\.woff2)\)', block)
        if url_match:
            font_url = url_match.group(1)
            if 'U+0600' in block:
                subset = 'arabic'
            else:
                subset = 'latin'
            filename = f'tajawal-{w}-{subset}.woff2'
            path = os.path.join(base_dir, filename)
            print(f'Downloading {filename}...')
            req2 = urllib.request.Request(font_url, headers={'User-Agent': ua})
            data = urllib.request.urlopen(req2).read()
            with open(path, 'wb') as f:
                f.write(data)
            print(f'  Saved {len(data)} bytes')

print('Done!')
```
