### 31. `fast_deploy.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Fast Deployment - Compress, Upload, Extract, Configure
"""

import paramiko
import zipfile
import os
import sys
import time
import io

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
LOCAL_PATH = r"c:\Users\IT\Desktop\online_4-main\attendance-laravel"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

# Skip these
SKIP_DIRS  = {".git", ".venv", "node_modules", "vendor", "storage"}
SKIP_FILES = {
    "deploy.sh", "deploy_automated.py", "deploy_v2.py", "full_deploy.py",
    "fast_deploy.py", "git-deploy.sh", "deployment.log", "nginx.conf",
    ".env.production", "setup_database.sql", "DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md",
    "SCRIPTS_DOCUMENTATION.md", "QUICK_DEPLOY.md", "START_HERE.md",
    "DEPLOYMENT_COMPLETE.md", "FINAL_STEPS_AR.md", "supervisor-attendance.conf",
    "backup.sh", "update.sh", "health-check.sh",
}

def log(msg):
    print(msg)
    sys.stdout.flush()

def connect():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)
    return ssh

def run(ssh, command, show=True, timeout=600):
    stdin, stdout, stderr = ssh.exec_command(command, timeout=timeout)
    out = stdout.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
    err = stderr.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
    exit_code = stdout.channel.recv_exit_status()
    if show and out.strip():
        log(out.strip()[:1000])
    if show and err.strip() and "warning" not in err.lower():
        log("[!] " + err.strip()[:400])
    return exit_code == 0, out, err

def create_zip():
    log("[*] Creating application archive...")
    buf = io.BytesIO()
    file_count = 0

    with zipfile.ZipFile(buf, "w", zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED, compresslevel=6) as zf:
        for root, dirs, files in os.walk(LOCAL_PATH):
            # Filter directories
            dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if d not in SKIP_DIRS]

            rel_root = os.path.relpath(root, LOCAL_PATH)
            if rel_root == ".":
                rel_root = ""

            for filename in files:
                if filename in SKIP_FILES:
                    continue
                full_path = os.path.join(root, filename)
                archive_name = os.path.join(rel_root, filename) if rel_root else filename
                archive_name = archive_name.replace("\\", "/")

                try:
                    zf.write(full_path, archive_name)
                    file_count += 1
                    if file_count % 50 == 0:
                        log("   Compressed %d files..." % file_count)
                except Exception as ex:
                    log("   Skip %s: %s" % (filename, str(ex)[:50]))

    size_mb = len(buf.getvalue()) / 1024 / 1024
    log("[+] Archive created: %.1f MB, %d files" % (size_mb, file_count))
    return buf.getvalue()

def main():
    log("\n" + "="*60)
    log("FAST DEPLOYMENT - Laravel Attendance")
    log("="*60 + "\n")

    # --- STEP 1: Create archive ---
    log("[1/8] Creating application archive...")
    zip_data = create_zip()

    # --- STEP 2: Connect ---
    log("\n[2/8] Connecting to VPS...")
    ssh = connect()
    log("[+] Connected to %s" % HOST)

    # --- STEP 3: Prepare remote directory ---
    log("\n[3/8] Preparing server directory...")
    run(ssh, "rm -rf %s && mkdir -p %s" % (REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH), show=False)
    log("[+] Directory ready!")

    # --- STEP 4: Upload ---
    log("\n[4/8] Uploading archive (%.1f MB)..." % (len(zip_data) / 1024 / 1024))
    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
    remote_zip = "/tmp/attendance_app.zip"
    sftp.putfo(io.BytesIO(zip_data), remote_zip)
    sftp.close()
    log("[+] Upload complete!")

    # --- STEP 5: Extract ---
    log("\n[5/8] Extracting archive on server...")
    run(ssh, "apt-get install -y unzip > /dev/null 2>&1")
    run(ssh, "cd %s && unzip -o /tmp/attendance_app.zip > /dev/null 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "rm -f /tmp/attendance_app.zip", show=False)

    # Create required storage directories
    run(ssh, """mkdir -p %s/storage/logs %s/storage/app/public \
    %s/storage/framework/cache %s/storage/framework/sessions \
    %s/storage/framework/views %s/bootstrap/cache""" % (
        REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH,
        REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH
    ), show=False)
    log("[+] Files extracted!")

    # --- STEP 6: Install dependencies ---
    log("\n[6/8] Installing PHP dependencies...")
    ok, out, err = run(ssh, "cd %s && composer install --optimize-autoloader --no-dev --no-interaction 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, timeout=300)
    if "Nothing to install" in out or "Package operations" in out or ok:
        log("[+] PHP dependencies installed!")
    else:
        log("[!] Composer: " + (err[:200] if err else out[:200]))

    # --- STEP 7: Configure App ---
    log("\n[7/8] Configuring application...")

    # Create .env from existing one but update settings
    ok, current_env, _ = run(ssh, "cat %s/.env 2>/dev/null || cat %s/.env.example 2>/dev/null" % (REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH), show=False)
    
    env_content = """APP_NAME=Attendance
APP_ENV=production
APP_KEY=
APP_DEBUG=false
APP_URL=http://{ip}

LOG_CHANNEL=stack
LOG_LEVEL=error

DB_CONNECTION=mysql
DB_HOST=127.0.0.1
DB_PORT=3306
DB_DATABASE=attendance_db
DB_USERNAME=attendance_user
DB_PASSWORD=Goolbx512@@@@

BROADCAST_DRIVER=log
CACHE_DRIVER=file
FILESYSTEM_DISK=local
QUEUE_CONNECTION=sync
SESSION_DRIVER=file
SESSION_LIFETIME=120

REDIS_HOST=127.0.0.1
REDIS_PASSWORD=null
REDIS_PORT=6379

MAIL_MAILER=log
""".format(ip=HOST)

    # Write .env file
    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
    with sftp.file(REMOTE_PATH + "/.env", "w") as f:
        f.write(env_content)
    sftp.close()

    # Generate APP_KEY
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan key:generate --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)

    # Create storage link
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan storage:link --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)

    # Fix permissions
    run(ssh, "chown -R www-data:www-data %s" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "chmod -R 755 %s" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "chmod -R 775 %s/storage %s/bootstrap/cache" % (REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH), show=False)

    # Run migrations
    log("   Running database migrations...")
    ok, out, err = run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan migrate --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    if ok:
        log("[+] Migrations OK!")
    else:
        log("[!] Migration output above")

    # Optimize
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan route:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan view:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    log("[+] Application configured and optimized!")

    # --- STEP 8: Configure Nginx ---
    log("\n[8/8] Configuring Nginx...")
    nginx_config = """server {{
    listen 80;
    listen [::]:80;
    server_name {ip} _;
    root {path}/public;
    index index.php index.html;

    access_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_access.log;
    error_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log;

    client_max_body_size 100M;

    add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN always;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff always;
    server_tokens off;

    location / {{
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.php?$query_string;
    }}

    location ~ \\.php$ {{
        fastcgi_split_path_info ^(.+\\.php)(/.+)$;
        fastcgi_pass unix:/run/php/php8.2-fpm.sock;
        fastcgi_index index.php;
        include fastcgi_params;
        fastcgi_param SCRIPT_FILENAME $document_root$fastcgi_script_name;
        fastcgi_param PATH_INFO $fastcgi_path_info;
    }}

    location ~ /\\.ht {{
        deny all;
    }}

    location ~* \\.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|ico|css|js|svg|woff|woff2|ttf|eot)$ {{
        expires 365d;
        add_header Cache-Control "public";
    }}
}}
""".format(ip=HOST, path=REMOTE_PATH)

    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
    with sftp.file("/etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance", "w") as f:
        f.write(nginx_config)
    sftp.close()

    run(ssh, "rm -f /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/default", show=False)
    run(ssh, "ln -sf /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/attendance", show=False)
    ok, out, err = run(ssh, "nginx -t 2>&1")
    if ok:
        log("[+] Nginx config is valid!")
        run(ssh, "systemctl restart nginx", show=False)
        run(ssh, "systemctl restart php8.2-fpm", show=False)
        log("[+] Nginx restarted!")
    else:
        log("[!] Nginx config error - check above")

    # --- FINAL CHECK ---
    log("\n" + "="*60)
    log("CHECKING APPLICATION...")
    log("="*60)
    run(ssh, "systemctl is-active nginx && echo 'Nginx: RUNNING' || echo 'Nginx: STOPPED'")
    run(ssh, "systemctl is-active php8.2-fpm && echo 'PHP-FPM: RUNNING' || echo 'PHP-FPM: STOPPED'")
    run(ssh, "systemctl is-active mysql && echo 'MySQL: RUNNING' || echo 'MySQL: STOPPED'")
    run(ssh, "ls %s/public/" % REMOTE_PATH)
    run(ssh, "curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'HTTP Status: %%{http_code}' http://localhost/")

    log("\n" + "="*60)
    log("[+] DEPLOYMENT COMPLETE!")
    log("="*60)
    log("")
    log("Your app is now live at:")
    log("   http://%s" % HOST)
    log("")
    log("To access admin panel:")
    log("   http://%s/admin" % HOST)
    log("")
    log("Logs:")
    log("   SSH: ssh root@%s" % HOST)
    log("   Nginx: /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log")
    log("   Laravel: %s/storage/logs/laravel.log" % REMOTE_PATH)
    log("="*60)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 32. `final_check.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Final verification of the deployed application"""
import paramiko

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, timeout=60, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(timeout)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out: print(out[:800])
            if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower() and "notice" not in err.lower():
                print("ERR:", err[:400])
        return out, err

    print("="*55)
    print("  FINAL APPLICATION STATUS CHECK")
    print("="*55)

    print("\n[1] HTTP responses:")
    out, _ = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Main page: %{http_code}' http://localhost/")
    out2, _ = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Login page: %{http_code}' http://localhost/login")
    out3, _ = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Admin page: %{http_code}' http://localhost/admin")
    out4, _ = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'API health: %{http_code}' http://localhost/api/health 2>/dev/null || echo 'N/A'")

    print("\n[2] Services status:")
    r("systemctl is-active nginx php8.3-fpm mysql redis-server")

    print("\n[3] Database tables count:")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SELECT COUNT(*) as tables FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema=\"attendance_db\";' 2>/dev/null")

    print("\n[4] Admin users in DB:")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SELECT name, email, created_at FROM admins LIMIT 5;' 2>/dev/null")

    print("\n[5] Storage & permissions:")
    r("ls -la %s/storage/logs/" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("ls -la %s/storage/framework/cache/ 2>/dev/null | head -5" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[6] Laravel version & environment:")
    r("cd %s && php artisan --version" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan env" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[7] Last Laravel log entries:")
    out, _ = r("tail -5 %s/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null || echo 'No log file yet'" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[8] Disk usage:")
    r("du -sh %s/" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("df -h / | tail -1")

    print("\n" + "="*55)
    print("  DEPLOYMENT COMPLETE!")
    print("="*55)
    print("URL:   http://%s" % HOST)
    print("Login: http://%s/login" % HOST)
    print("Admin: http://%s/admin" % HOST)
    print("")
    print("Default credentials (from seeders):")
    print("  Email:    admin@attendance.com")
    print("  Password: password")
    print("="*55)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 33. `finish_deploy.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Final configuration - Fix Nginx and run migrations
"""
import paramiko

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"  
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

nginx_config = r"""server {
    listen 80;
    listen [::]:80;
    server_name 187.77.173.160 _;
    root /var/www/attendance/public;
    index index.php index.html;

    access_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_access.log;
    error_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log;

    client_max_body_size 100M;

    add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN always;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff always;
    server_tokens off;

    location / {
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.php?$query_string;
    }

    location ~ \.php$ {
        fastcgi_split_path_info ^(.+\.php)(/.+)$;
        fastcgi_pass unix:/run/php/php8.3-fpm.sock;
        fastcgi_index index.php;
        include fastcgi_params;
        fastcgi_param SCRIPT_FILENAME $document_root$fastcgi_script_name;
        fastcgi_param PATH_INFO $fastcgi_path_info;
    }

    location ~ /\.ht {
        deny all;
    }

    location ~* \.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|ico|css|js|svg|woff|woff2|ttf|eot)$ {
        expires 365d;
        add_header Cache-Control "public";
    }
}
"""

def main():
    print("[*] Connecting to %s..." % HOST)
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)
    print("[+] Connected!")

    def r(cmd, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(300)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out:
                print(out[:800])
            if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "hint" not in err.lower():
                print("ERR:", err[:400])
        return out, err

    print()
    print("[1] Writing Nginx config with PHP 8.3...")
    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
    with sftp.file("/etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance", "w") as f:
        f.write(nginx_config)
    sftp.close()

    r("rm -f /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/default", show=False)
    r("ln -sf /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/attendance", show=False)
    out, err = r("nginx -t 2>&1")
    if "successful" in (out + err).lower():
        print("[+] Nginx config valid!")
        r("systemctl restart nginx", show=False)
        print("[+] Nginx restarted!")
    else:
        print("[!] Nginx config error - check above output")

    print()
    print("[2] Ensuring PHP-FPM 8.3 is running...")
    r("systemctl start php8.3-fpm", show=False)
    r("systemctl enable php8.3-fpm", show=False)
    out, _ = r("systemctl is-active php8.3-fpm", show=False)
    print("PHP-FPM 8.3: " + out)

    print()
    print("[3] Running database migrations...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan migrate --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print()
    print("[4] Running database seeders...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan db:seed --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print()
    print("[5] Optimizing application...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    r("cd %s && php artisan view:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    print("[+] Application optimized!")

    print()
    print("[6] Testing HTTP response...")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'HTTP Status: %{http_code}' http://localhost/ 2>&1")

    print()
    print("[7] Services status check...")
    r("echo 'Nginx:' $(systemctl is-active nginx)")
    r("echo 'PHP-FPM:' $(systemctl is-active php8.3-fpm)")
    r("echo 'MySQL:' $(systemctl is-active mysql)")

    print()
    print("[8] Checking Laravel app...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan --version 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:list --compact 2>&1 | head -20" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print()
    print("=" * 50)
    print("[+] DEPLOYMENT COMPLETE!")
    print("=" * 50)
    print()
    print("Application URL:  http://%s" % HOST)
    print("Admin Panel:      http://%s/admin" % HOST)
    print("API Base:         http://%s/api" % HOST)
    print()
    print("SSH access:       ssh root@%s" % HOST)
    print("App path:         %s" % REMOTE_PATH)
    print("Nginx log:        /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log")
    print("Laravel log:      %s/storage/logs/laravel.log" % REMOTE_PATH)
    print("=" * 50)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 34. `fix_admin.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Fix Redis and check/reset admin credentials"""
import paramiko

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, timeout=90, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(timeout)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out: print(out[:1000])
            if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower() and "notice" not in err.lower():
                print("ERR:", err[:500])
        return out, err

    # 1. Check current admin
    print("[1] Current admin user...")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SELECT id, username, full_name, email FROM admins;' 2>/dev/null")

    # 2. Check DatabaseSeeder and AdminFactory
    print("\n[2] Check seeder/factory for admin credentials...")
    r("grep -r 'password\\|username\\|admin' %s/database/seeders/ 2>/dev/null | head -20" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # 3. Fix Redis - check why it's failing
    print("\n[3] Redis error details...")
    r("journalctl -u redis-server -n 20 --no-pager 2>/dev/null | tail -15")
    r("redis-server --version 2>/dev/null || echo 'redis not found'")

    # Try installing redis if needed
    print("\n[4] Fixing Redis...")
    r("apt-get install -y redis-server 2>&1 | tail -5")
    r("systemctl daemon-reload")
    r("systemctl start redis-server 2>&1")
    out, _ = r("systemctl is-active redis-server")
    print("Redis status:", out)

    # 5. Check the Admin model password hashing method
    print("\n[5] Check Admin model auth method...")
    r("cat %s/app/Models/Admin.php 2>/dev/null" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # 6. Create/reset admin password using PHP
    print("\n[6] Resetting admin password using artisan tinker...")
    tinker_cmd = """cd %s && php artisan tinker --execute="
\$admin = \\\\App\\\\Models\\\\Admin::first();
if (\$admin) {
    echo 'Admin found: ' . \$admin->username . ' / ' . \$admin->email . PHP_EOL;
} else {
    echo 'No admin found' . PHP_EOL;
}
" 2>&1""" % REMOTE_PATH
    r(tinker_cmd)

    # 7. Try to get admin hashing method from the model, then set password
    print("\n[7] Setting admin password to known value...")
    tinker_cmd2 = """cd %s && php artisan tinker --execute="
\$admin = \\\\App\\\\Models\\\\Admin::first();
if (\$admin) {
    \$admin->password_hash = bcrypt('Admin@123456');
    \$admin->save();
    echo 'Password updated for: ' . \$admin->username . PHP_EOL;
    echo 'Email: ' . \$admin->email . PHP_EOL;
} else {
    \\\\App\\\\Models\\\\Admin::create([
        'username' => 'admin',
        'full_name' => 'System Admin',
        'email' => 'admin@attendance.com',
        'password_hash' => bcrypt('Admin@123456'),
    ]);
    echo 'New admin created!' . PHP_EOL;
}
" 2>&1""" % REMOTE_PATH
    r(tinker_cmd2)

    print("\n[8] Final admin check...")
    r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SELECT id, username, full_name, email FROM admins;' 2>/dev/null")

    print("\n[9] Testing admin login page...")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Admin login: %{http_code}' http://localhost/admin/login")

    print("\n" + "="*55)
    print("  ACCESS INFORMATION")
    print("="*55)
    print("Admin Panel: http://%s/admin/login" % HOST)
    print("Password:    Admin@123456")
    print("="*55)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 35. `fix_db.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Fix MySQL user and run migrations"""
import paramiko

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(120)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out:
                print(out[:600])
            if err and "warning" not in err.lower():
                print("ERR:", err[:300])
        return out, err

    print("[+] Connected to server")

    # Fix MySQL user
    print("\n[1] Fixing MySQL user...")
    r("sudo mysql -e \"DROP USER IF EXISTS 'attendance_user'@'localhost';\"", show=False)
    r("sudo mysql -e \"CREATE USER 'attendance_user'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED WITH mysql_native_password BY 'Goolbx512@@@@';\"", show=False)
    r("sudo mysql -e \"GRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON attendance_db.* TO 'attendance_user'@'localhost';\"", show=False)
    r("sudo mysql -e \"FLUSH PRIVILEGES;\"", show=False)
    print("[+] MySQL user recreated!")

    # Test MySQL connection
    print("\n[2] Testing MySQL connection...")
    out, err = r("mysql -u attendance_user -pGoolbx512@@@@ attendance_db -e 'SHOW TABLES;' 2>&1")
    if err and "access denied" in err.lower():
        print("[!] Still access denied - trying to fix...")
        r("sudo mysql -e \"ALTER USER 'attendance_user'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED BY 'Goolbx512@@@@';\"", show=False)
        r("sudo mysql -e \"FLUSH PRIVILEGES;\"", show=False)
    else:
        print("[+] MySQL connection OK!")

    # Run migrations
    print("\n[3] Running migrations...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan migrate --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Run seeders
    print("\n[4] Running seeders...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan db:seed --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Optimize
    print("\n[5] Optimizing...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    r("cd %s && php artisan view:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    print("[+] Optimized!")

    # Test HTTP
    print("\n[6] Testing application HTTP response...")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'HTTP Status: %{http_code}' http://localhost/ 2>&1")

    print("\n[7] Services status:")
    r("echo nginx=$(systemctl is-active nginx)")
    r("echo php-fpm=$(systemctl is-active php8.3-fpm)")
    r("echo mysql=$(systemctl is-active mysql)")

    print("\n" + "=" * 50)
    print("[+] DONE! App is live at: http://%s" % HOST)
    print("=" * 50)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 36. `fix_indexphp.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Upload fixed index.php and verify app works"""
import paramiko
import io

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(60)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out: print(out[:600])
            if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower():
                print("ERR:", err[:300])
        return out, err

    print("[+] Connected!")

    # Read the fixed local index.php
    local_file = r"c:\Users\IT\Desktop\online_4-main\attendance-laravel\public\index.php"
    with open(local_file, "rb") as f:
        content = f.read()

    print("[1] Uploading fixed public/index.php...")
    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
    sftp.putfo(io.BytesIO(content), REMOTE_PATH + "/public/index.php")
    sftp.close()
    print("[+] File uploaded!")

    print("\n[2] Verifying the fix on server...")
    r("grep -n 'vendor/autoload' %s/public/index.php" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("grep -n 'bootstrap/app' %s/public/index.php" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[3] Clearing cache to apply changes...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)

    print("\n[4] Testing HTTP response...")
    out, _ = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'HTTP %{http_code}' http://localhost/")

    if "200" in out or "302" in out or "301" in out:
        print("\n[+] SUCCESS! Application is responding correctly!")
    else:
        print("\n[!] Still getting errors. Checking logs...")
        r("tail -20 /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log 2>/dev/null")
        r("tail -20 /var/www/attendance/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null | tail -20")

    print("\n[5] Checking API routes...")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'API HTTP: %{http_code}' http://localhost/api/")

    print("\n" + "="*50)
    print("Application URL: http://%s" % HOST)
    print("="*50)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 37. `fix_redis.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Fix Redis config and do final test"""
import paramiko
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, timeout=90, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(timeout)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out: print(out[:800])
            if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower() and "notice" not in err.lower():
                print("ERR:", err[:400])
        return out, err

    # 1. Check Redis actual error
    print("[1] Redis actual error...")
    r("redis-server /etc/redis/redis.conf --loglevel verbose 2>&1 | head -10 &")
    time.sleep(2)
    r("journalctl -u redis-server -n 5 --no-pager 2>/dev/null | grep -i 'error\\|fatal\\|warn' | head -5")

    # Fix Redis: comment out IPv6 binding
    print("\n[2] Fixing Redis config (IPv6 bind issue)...")
    r("cp /etc/redis/redis.conf /etc/redis/redis.conf.bak")
    # Comment out the default bind and add only IPv4
    r("sed -i 's/^bind 127.0.0.1 -::1/bind 127.0.0.1/' /etc/redis/redis.conf")
    r("grep '^bind' /etc/redis/redis.conf")

    # Try starting Redis again
    r("systemctl stop redis-server 2>/dev/null; true")
    time.sleep(1)
    r("systemctl start redis-server 2>&1")
    time.sleep(3)
    out, _ = r("systemctl is-active redis-server")
    print("Redis status:", out)

    if out == "active":
        print("[+] Redis is now ACTIVE!")
        # Update .env to use Redis for cache
        r("sed -i 's/CACHE_DRIVER=file/CACHE_DRIVER=file/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)  # keep file driver, Redis for session only
        r("redis-cli ping")
    else:
        print("[!] Redis still failing - checking detailed error...")
        r("redis-server --test-memory 64 2>&1 | head -5 || true")
        r("redis-server /etc/redis/redis.conf 2>&1 | head -10 &")
        time.sleep(2)
        r("pgrep -a redis")

    # Clean caches
    print("\n[3] Refreshing application cache...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan view:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    # Final HTTP test
    print("\n[4] Final HTTP tests...")
    routes = [
        ("Main page",   "/"),
        ("Admin login", "/admin/login"),
        ("Admin panel", "/admin/dashboard"),
        ("Employee",    "/employee"),
        ("API health",  "/api/health"),
    ]
    for name, route in routes:
        out, _ = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'HTTP %{http_code}' http://localhost%s" % route, show=False)
        status = out.replace("HTTP ", "")
        ok = "[+]" if status in ["200", "302", "301"] else "[-]"
        print("  %s  %-15s %s" % (ok, name, status))

    print("\n" + "="*55)
    print("  DEPLOYMENT COMPLETE - FINAL SUMMARY")
    print("="*55)
    print("")
    print("Application URL:  http://%s" % HOST)
    print("Admin Panel:      http://%s/admin/login" % HOST)
    print("")
    print("Credentials:")
    print("  Username: admin")
    print("  Password: Admin@123456")
    print("")
    print("Database:")
    print("  Host:     localhost")
    print("  Name:     attendance_db")
    print("  User:     attendance_user")
    print("  Pass:     Goolbx512@@@@")
    print("="*55)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 38. `fix_redis2.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Fix Redis properly - check actual error and fix"""
import paramiko
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, timeout=30, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(timeout)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out: print(out[:800])
            if err: print("ERR:", err[:400])
        return out, err

    print("[1] Get Redis detailed error...")
    r("journalctl -u redis-server --no-pager -n 30 2>/dev/null | tail -20")

    print("\n[2] Check if Redis runs manually with default config...")
    r("redis-server --daemonize yes --logfile /tmp/redis_test.log --port 6380 2>&1")
    time.sleep(2)
    r("cat /tmp/redis_test.log 2>/dev/null | head -20")
    r("redis-cli -p 6380 ping 2>/dev/null")
    r("pkill -f 'redis-server.*6380' 2>/dev/null || true")

    print("\n[3] Apply common Redis fixes...")
    # Fix overcommit memory warning (common issue)
    r("sysctl vm.overcommit_memory=1")
    r("echo 'vm.overcommit_memory = 1' >> /etc/sysctl.conf")
    # Fix transparent huge pages
    r("echo never > /sys/kernel/mm/transparent_hugepage/enabled 2>/dev/null || true")

    # Remove stale PID/socket files
    r("rm -f /var/run/redis/redis-server.pid 2>/dev/null || true")
    r("rm -f /run/redis/redis-server.pid 2>/dev/null || true")
    r("ls /var/run/redis/ 2>/dev/null || echo 'no /var/run/redis'")

    # Ensure correct directory permissions
    r("mkdir -p /var/log/redis /var/lib/redis")
    r("chown -R redis:redis /var/log/redis /var/lib/redis 2>/dev/null || true")

    # Check actual Redis config
    r("grep -E '^(bind|port|pidfile|logfile|daemonize|supervised|dir)' /etc/redis/redis.conf")

    print("\n[4] Try starting Redis now...")
    r("systemctl stop redis-server 2>/dev/null; true")
    time.sleep(1)
    r("systemctl start redis-server 2>&1")
    time.sleep(3)
    out, _ = r("systemctl is-active redis-server")
    print("Redis status:", out)

    if out == "active":
        print("[+] Redis is now ACTIVE!")
        r("redis-cli ping")
    else:
        # Try alternative: run redis directly
        print("[!] Trying alternative: start Redis directly (not via systemd)...")
        r("redis-server /etc/redis/redis.conf --daemonize yes 2>&1")
        time.sleep(2)
        out, _ = r("redis-cli ping 2>/dev/null")
        if out == "PONG":
            print("[+] Redis is running (manual start)!")
        else:
            print("[!] Redis unavailable - app will use file driver (OK for now)")
            # Make sure .env uses file driver
            r("grep 'CACHE_DRIVER\\|SESSION_DRIVER\\|QUEUE_CONNECTION' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[5] Final application test...")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Admin Login: %%{http_code}\\n' http://localhost/admin/login")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Main Page: %%{http_code}\\n' http://localhost/")

    print("\n" + "="*55)
    print("  FINAL ACCESS DETAILS")
    print("="*55)
    print("Admin URL:  http://%s/admin/login" % HOST)
    print("Username:   admin")
    print("Password:   Admin@123456")
    print("")
    print("Or try original seeder password: Admin@1234")
    print("="*55)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 39. `fix_redis3.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Fix Redis - pidfile directory and systemd supervised mode"""
import paramiko
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, timeout=30, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(timeout)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out: print(out[:800])
            if err: print("ERR:", err[:400])
        return out, err

    print("[1] Checking Redis config issue...")
    # The issue: daemonize=yes conflicts with supervised=systemd
    # systemd expects Redis to NOT daemonize when using supervised mode
    out, _ = r("grep -E '^(supervised|daemonize)' /etc/redis/redis.conf")

    print("\n[2] Fix Redis config - supervised systemd needs daemonize no...")
    # Change supervised to auto (handles both cases)
    r("sed -i 's/^supervised .*/supervised auto/' /etc/redis/redis.conf")
    # Change daemonize to no when supervised=auto (systemd handles the process)
    r("sed -i 's/^daemonize yes/daemonize no/' /etc/redis/redis.conf")

    # Create the pidfile directory
    r("mkdir -p /run/redis")
    r("chown redis:redis /run/redis 2>/dev/null || true")
    r("chmod 755 /run/redis")

    # Check if logfile is writable
    r("touch /var/log/redis/redis-server.log 2>/dev/null; true")
    r("chown redis:redis /var/log/redis/ 2>/dev/null; true")

    r("grep -E '^(supervised|daemonize|pidfile|bind|port)' /etc/redis/redis.conf")

    print("\n[3] Check systemd unit file for Redis...")
    r("cat /lib/systemd/system/redis-server.service 2>/dev/null | grep -E 'Type|ExecStart|User' | head -10")

    print("\n[4] Restart Redis with fixed config...")
    r("systemctl daemon-reload")
    r("systemctl stop redis-server 2>/dev/null; true")
    time.sleep(2)
    r("systemctl start redis-server")
    time.sleep(3)
    out, _ = r("systemctl is-active redis-server")
    print("Redis status:", out)

    if out == "active":
        print("[+] Redis is now RUNNING!")
        r("redis-cli ping")
    else:
        print("[x] Redis still failing - last log...")
        r("cat /var/log/redis/redis-server.log 2>/dev/null | tail -15")
        r("journalctl -u redis-server -n 10 --no-pager 2>/dev/null | grep -v '^--'")
        print("\n[!] App will work fine with file driver - Redis not critical")

    print("\n[5] Final verification...")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Admin Login: %%{http_code}' http://localhost/admin/login")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Main Page: %%{http_code}' http://localhost/")

    print("\n" + "="*55)
    print("APPLICATION IS LIVE!")
    print("="*55)
    print("  URL:      http://%s/admin/login" % HOST)
    print("  Username: admin")
    print("  Password: Admin@123456")
    print("="*55)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 40. `fix_redis4.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Diagnose Redis with detailed log check"""
import paramiko
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, t=20):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(t)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        if out: print(out[:600])
        if err: print("ERR:", err[:300])
        return out

    print("=== Redis Log ===")
    r("cat /var/log/redis/redis-server.log 2>/dev/null | tail -20 || echo 'no log file'")

    print("\n=== Check /run/redis dir ===")
    r("ls -la /run/redis 2>/dev/null || echo 'dir missing'")
    r("ls -la /run/ | grep -i redis || echo 'nothing'")

    print("\n=== tmpfiles.d for Redis ===")
    r("find /usr/lib/tmpfiles.d /etc/tmpfiles.d -name '*redis*' 2>/dev/null -exec cat {} \\;")

    print("\n=== Disable pidfile in config ===")
    r("sed -i 's|^pidfile.*|pidfile \"\"|' /etc/redis/redis.conf")
    r("grep 'pidfile' /etc/redis/redis.conf")

    print("\n=== Start Redis now ===")
    r("systemctl stop redis-server 2>/dev/null || true")
    time.sleep(1)
    r("systemctl start redis-server")
    time.sleep(3)
    status = r("systemctl is-active redis-server")
    print("Status:", status)

    if status == "active":
        print("[+] Redis ACTIVE!")
        r("redis-cli ping")
    else:
        print("[!] Still failing, reading log...")
        r("cat /var/log/redis/redis-server.log 2>/dev/null | tail -15 || echo 'no log'")
        r("journalctl -u redis-server -n 5 --no-pager 2>/dev/null | grep -v '^--'")

        # Last resort: run Redis manually as daemon
        print("\n=== Manual Redis start ===")
        r("pkill redis-server 2>/dev/null || true")
        time.sleep(1)
        r("sudo -u redis /usr/bin/redis-server --port 6379 --daemonize yes --logfile /var/log/redis/redis.log --bind 127.0.0.1 2>&1")
        time.sleep(2)
        pong = r("redis-cli ping 2>/dev/null || echo 'no'")
        if pong == "PONG":
            print("[+] Redis running via manual start!")
        else:
            print("[!] Redis not available - app uses file driver, this is OK")

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 41. `fix_redis5.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Redis is running - just fix systemd conflict"""
import paramiko
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, t=20, show=True):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(t)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        if show:
            if out: print(out[:600])
            if err: print("ERR:", err[:300])
        return out

    print("[1] What is using port 6379?")
    r("ss -tlnp | grep 6379")
    r("fuser 6379/tcp 2>/dev/null || true")

    print("\n[2] Redis ping test...")
    out = r("redis-cli ping 2>/dev/null || echo 'no ping'")

    if out == "PONG":
        print("[+] Redis IS running and responding!")
    else:
        print("[!] Redis not responding")

    print("\n[3] Check Redis process...")
    r("pgrep -a redis-server 2>/dev/null || echo 'no process'")

    print("\n[4] Kill any stale Redis + clean start via systemd...")
    r("pkill -9 redis-server 2>/dev/null || true")
    time.sleep(2)
    r("systemctl daemon-reload")
    r("systemctl start redis-server")
    time.sleep(3)
    status = r("systemctl is-active redis-server")
    print("Redis status:", status)

    r("redis-cli ping 2>/dev/null || echo 'no ping'")

    print("\n[5] Update .env if Redis is working...")
    status = r("systemctl is-active redis-server", show=False)
    ping = r("redis-cli ping 2>/dev/null", show=False)
    if status == "active" or ping == "PONG":
        print("[+] Redis confirmed! Updating .env to use Redis cache...")
        r("sed -i 's/CACHE_DRIVER=file/CACHE_DRIVER=redis/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)
        r("sed -i 's/SESSION_DRIVER=file/SESSION_DRIVER=redis/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)
        r("cd %s && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1 | tail -3" % REMOTE_PATH, t=30)
        r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1 | tail -2" % REMOTE_PATH, t=30)

    print("\n[6] All services status...")
    r("systemctl is-active nginx php8.3-fpm mysql redis-server")

    print("\n[7] Final HTTP test...")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Admin login: %%{http_code}' http://localhost/admin/login")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w ' | Main page: %%{http_code}' http://localhost/")

    print("\n" + "="*55)
    print("  APPLICATION LIVE!")
    print("="*55)
    print("  http://%s/admin/login" % HOST)
    print("  Username: admin")
    print("  Password: Admin@123456")
    print("="*55)

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 42. `full_deploy.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Full Deployment Script - Upload all files + complete setup
"""

import paramiko
import os
import sys
import stat
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
LOCAL_PATH = r"c:\Users\IT\Desktop\online_4-main\attendance-laravel"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

# Files/folders to skip
SKIP = {
    ".git", ".venv", "node_modules", "vendor",
    "storage\\logs", "storage/logs",
    ".env.production", "deploy.sh", "deploy_automated.py",
    "deploy_v2.py", "full_deploy.py", "git-deploy.sh",
    "DEPLOYMENT_GUIDE_AR.md", "SCRIPTS_DOCUMENTATION.md",
    "QUICK_DEPLOY.md", "START_HERE.md", "DEPLOYMENT_COMPLETE.md",
    "FINAL_STEPS_AR.md", "deployment.log", "supervisor-attendance.conf",
    "backup.sh", "update.sh", "health-check.sh",
    "setup_database.sql",
}

def log(msg):
    print(msg)
    sys.stdout.flush()

def connect():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)
    return ssh

def run(ssh, command, show=True):
    stdin, stdout, stderr = ssh.exec_command(command)
    stdout.channel.settimeout(600)
    out = stdout.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
    err = stderr.read().decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
    if show and out.strip():
        log(out.strip()[:800])
    return stdout.channel.recv_exit_status() == 0, out, err

def upload_directory(sftp, local_dir, remote_dir):
    """Recursively upload directory"""
    try:
        sftp.mkdir(remote_dir)
    except:
        pass

    items = os.listdir(local_dir)
    total = len(items)
    for i, item in enumerate(items):
        if item in SKIP:
            continue
        local_item = os.path.join(local_dir, item)
        remote_item = remote_dir + "/" + item

        if os.path.isdir(local_item):
            # Skip storage/logs but allow storage/app, storage/framework
            if item == "logs" and local_dir.endswith("storage"):
                continue
            upload_directory(sftp, local_item, remote_item)
        else:
            try:
                sftp.put(local_item, remote_item)
                if i % 20 == 0:
                    log("   Uploaded %d/%d files in %s..." % (i, total, os.path.basename(local_dir)))
            except Exception as e:
                log("   Skip %s: %s" % (item, str(e)[:50]))

def main():
    log("\n" + "="*60)
    log("FULL DEPLOYMENT - Laravel Attendance App")
    log("="*60)
    log("Server: %s" % HOST)
    log("Remote: %s" % REMOTE_PATH)
    log("Local:  %s" % LOCAL_PATH)
    log("="*60 + "\n")

    # --- CONNECT ---
    log("[*] Connecting to VPS...")
    ssh = connect()
    log("[+] Connected!\n")

    # --- PREPARE REMOTE DIR ---
    log("[1] Preparing remote directory...")
    run(ssh, "rm -rf %s && mkdir -p %s" % (REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH), show=False)
    run(ssh, "mkdir -p %s/storage/logs %s/storage/app %s/storage/framework/cache %s/storage/framework/sessions %s/storage/framework/views %s/bootstrap/cache" % (
        REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH
    ), show=False)
    log("[+] Directory ready!")

    # --- UPLOAD FILES ---
    log("\n[2] Uploading application files (this may take a few minutes)...")
    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
    upload_directory(sftp, LOCAL_PATH, REMOTE_PATH)
    sftp.close()
    log("[+] Files uploaded!")

    # --- FIX PERMISSIONS ---
    log("\n[3] Fixing permissions...")
    run(ssh, "chown -R www-data:www-data %s" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "chmod -R 755 %s" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "chmod -R 775 %s/storage %s/bootstrap/cache" % (REMOTE_PATH, REMOTE_PATH), show=False)
    log("[+] Permissions set!")

    # --- INSTALL PHP DEPS ---
    log("\n[4] Installing Composer dependencies (no-dev)...")
    ok, out, err = run(ssh, "cd %s && composer install --optimize-autoloader --no-dev --no-interaction 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    if ok:
        log("[+] Composer dependencies installed!")
    else:
        log("[!] Composer warning (may still work): " + err[:300])

    # --- CONFIGURE .ENV ---
    log("\n[5] Configuring .env file...")
    env_content = """APP_NAME=Attendance
APP_ENV=production
APP_KEY=
APP_DEBUG=false
APP_URL=http://%s

LOG_CHANNEL=stack
LOG_LEVEL=error

DB_CONNECTION=mysql
DB_HOST=127.0.0.1
DB_PORT=3306
DB_DATABASE=attendance_db
DB_USERNAME=attendance_user
DB_PASSWORD=Goolbx512@@@@

BROADCAST_DRIVER=log
CACHE_DRIVER=file
FILESYSTEM_DISK=local
QUEUE_CONNECTION=sync
SESSION_DRIVER=file
SESSION_LIFETIME=120

REDIS_HOST=127.0.0.1
REDIS_PASSWORD=null
REDIS_PORT=6379
""" % HOST

    # Write .env to remote
    run(ssh, "cat > %s/.env << 'ENVEOF'\n%sENVEOF" % (REMOTE_PATH, env_content), show=False)
    log("[+] .env file created!")

    # --- GENERATE APP KEY ---
    log("\n[6] Generating application key...")
    ok, out, err = run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan key:generate --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    log("[+] App key generated!")

    # --- RUN MIGRATIONS ---
    log("\n[7] Running database migrations...")
    ok, out, err = run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan migrate --force 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    if ok:
        log("[+] Migrations completed!")
    else:
        log("[!] Migration output: " + out[:400])

    # --- OPTIMIZE ---
    log("\n[8] Optimizing application...")
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan route:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan view:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    run(ssh, "cd %s && php artisan storage:link 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, show=False)
    log("[+] Application optimized!")

    # --- CONFIGURE NGINX ---
    log("\n[9] Configuring Nginx...")
    nginx_config = """server {
    listen 80;
    listen [::]:80;
    server_name %s;
    root %s/public;
    index index.php;

    access_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_access.log;
    error_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log;

    client_max_body_size 100M;

    add_header X-Frame-Options SAMEORIGIN;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff;

    location / {
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.php?$query_string;
    }

    location ~ \\.php$ {
        include snippets/fastcgi-php.conf;
        fastcgi_pass unix:/run/php/php8.2-fpm.sock;
        fastcgi_param SCRIPT_FILENAME $document_root$fastcgi_script_name;
    }

    location ~ /\\. {
        deny all;
    }
}
""" % (HOST, REMOTE_PATH)

    run(ssh, "cat > /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance << 'NGINXEOF'\n%sNGINXEOF" % nginx_config, show=False)
    run(ssh, "rm -f /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/default", show=False)
    run(ssh, "ln -sf /etc/nginx/sites-available/attendance /etc/nginx/sites-enabled/", show=False)
    ok, out, err = run(ssh, "nginx -t 2>&1")
    if "successful" in out or "successful" in err:
        log("[+] Nginx config valid!")
    run(ssh, "systemctl restart nginx", show=False)
    run(ssh, "systemctl restart php8.2-fpm", show=False)
    log("[+] Nginx configured and restarted!")

    # --- FINAL STATUS CHECK ---
    log("\n[10] Final status check...")
    log("\n--- Nginx ---")
    run(ssh, "systemctl is-active nginx")
    log("--- PHP-FPM ---")
    run(ssh, "systemctl is-active php8.2-fpm")
    log("--- MySQL ---")
    run(ssh, "systemctl is-active mysql")

    log("\n" + "="*60)
    log("[+] DEPLOYMENT COMPLETE!")
    log("="*60)
    log("\nYour application is now live at:")
    log("   http://%s" % HOST)
    log("\nAdmin Panel (if exists):")
    log("   http://%s/admin" % HOST)
    log("\nAPI Base URL:")
    log("   http://%s/api" % HOST)
    log("\nDatabase info:")
    log("   DB: attendance_db | User: attendance_user")
    log("="*60 + "\n")

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 43. `git-deploy.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
# Git Deployment Script - Upload application to Hostinger VPS

# Configuration
REMOTE_HOST="187.77.173.160"
REMOTE_USER="root"
REMOTE_PATH="/var/www/attendance"
LOCAL_PATH="."

echo "========================================"
echo "Git Deployment to VPS"
echo "========================================"

# Add Git remote if not exists
if ! git remote | grep -q "production"; then
    echo "[*] Adding production remote..."
    git remote add production ssh://${REMOTE_USER}@${REMOTE_HOST}${REMOTE_PATH}
else
    echo "[*] Production remote already configured"
fi

# Push to production
echo "[*] Pushing code to production..."
git push -u production main

if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then
    echo ""
    echo "[+] Code pushed successfully!"
    echo ""
    echo "[*] Next steps on the server:"
    echo "    1. cd /var/www/attendance"
    echo "    2. composer install --no-dev --optimize-autoloader"
    echo "    3. npm install && npm run build"
    echo "    4. php artisan migrate --force"
    echo "    5. php artisan optimize"
else
    echo "[!] Push failed!"
    exit 1
fi
```

### 44. `health-check.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# Health Check Script - Monitor application health
# Schedule with cron: */5 * * * * /var/www/attendance/health-check.sh

APP_DIR="/var/www/attendance"
LOG_FILE="/var/log/attendance-health.log"

echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] Starting health check..." >> $LOG_FILE

# Check if Nginx is running
if ! sudo systemctl is-active --quiet nginx; then
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ERROR: Nginx is not running" >> $LOG_FILE
    sudo systemctl restart nginx
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] Nginx restarted" >> $LOG_FILE
else
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ✓ Nginx running" >> $LOG_FILE
fi

# Check if PHP-FPM is running
if ! sudo systemctl is-active --quiet php8.2-fpm; then
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ERROR: PHP-FPM is not running" >> $LOG_FILE
    sudo systemctl restart php8.2-fpm
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] PHP-FPM restarted" >> $LOG_FILE
else
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ✓ PHP-FPM running" >> $LOG_FILE
fi

# Check if MySQL is running
if ! sudo systemctl is-active --quiet mysql; then
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ERROR: MySQL is not running" >> $LOG_FILE
    sudo systemctl restart mysql
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] MySQL restarted" >> $LOG_FILE
else
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ✓ MySQL running" >> $LOG_FILE
fi

# Check disk space
DISK_USAGE=$(df /var/www/attendance | awk 'NR==2 {print $5}' | sed 's/%//')
if [ $DISK_USAGE -gt 90 ]; then
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] WARNING: Disk usage is ${DISK_USAGE}%" >> $LOG_FILE
else
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ✓ Disk usage: ${DISK_USAGE}%" >> $LOG_FILE
fi

# Check application logs for errors
if sudo tail -100 $APP_DIR/storage/logs/laravel.log | grep -q "ERROR\|CRITICAL"; then
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] WARNING: Errors found in application logs" >> $LOG_FILE
else
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ✓ Application logs clean" >> $LOG_FILE
fi

# HTTP check
HTTP_STATUS=$(curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" https://your-domain.com --connect-timeout 5)
if [ "$HTTP_STATUS" = "200" ] || [ "$HTTP_STATUS" = "301" ] || [ "$HTTP_STATUS" = "302" ]; then
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ✓ Application responding (HTTP $HTTP_STATUS)" >> $LOG_FILE
else
    echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] ERROR: Application not responding (HTTP $HTTP_STATUS)" >> $LOG_FILE
fi

echo "[$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')] Health check completed" >> $LOG_FILE
echo "" >> $LOG_FILE
```

### 45. `nginx.conf`

```ini
server {
    listen 80;
    listen [::]:80;
    server_name your-domain.com www.your-domain.com;

    # Redirect HTTP to HTTPS
    return 301 https://$server_name$request_uri;
}

server {
    listen 443 ssl http2;
    listen [::]:443 ssl http2;

    server_name your-domain.com www.your-domain.com;
    root /var/www/attendance/public;
    index index.php;

    # SSL certificates (update after running certbot)
    # ssl_certificate /etc/letsencrypt/live/your-domain.com/fullchain.pem;
    # ssl_certificate_key /etc/letsencrypt/live/your-domain.com/privkey.pem;
    # ssl_protocols TLSv1.2 TLSv1.3;
    # ssl_ciphers HIGH:!aNULL:!MD5;
    # ssl_prefer_server_ciphers on;

    # Logs
    access_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_access.log;
    error_log /var/log/nginx/attendance_error.log;

    # Gzip compression
    gzip on;
    gzip_vary on;
    gzip_min_length 1000;
    gzip_types text/plain text/css text/xml text/javascript
               application/x-javascript application/xml+rss
               application/json application/javascript;

    # Security headers
    add_header X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN" always;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff" always;
    add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;
    add_header Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" always;

    # Hide nginx version
    server_tokens off;

    client_max_body_size 100M;

    # Main location block
    location / {
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.php?$query_string;
    }

    # PHP handling
    location ~ \.php$ {
        include snippets/fastcgi-php.conf;
        fastcgi_pass unix:/run/php/php8.2-fpm.sock;
        fastcgi_param SCRIPT_FILENAME $document_root$fastcgi_script_name;
        fastcgi_param PATH_INFO $fastcgi_path_info;
    }

    # Cache static assets
    location ~* \.(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|ico|css|js|svg|woff|woff2|ttf|eot)$ {
        expires 365d;
        add_header Cache-Control "public, immutable";
    }

    # Deny access to hidden files
    location ~ /\. {
        deny all;
    }

    # Deny access to sensitive Laravel files
    location ~ /(storage|bootstrap|config|\.env|composer\.) {
        deny all;
    }
}
```

### 47. `phpunit.xml`

```xml
<phpunit xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance"

         bootstrap="vendor/autoload.php"
         colors="true"

            <directory>tests/Unit</directory>
        </testsuite>

            <directory>tests/Feature</directory>
        </testsuite>
    </testsuites>
    <source>
        <include>
            <directory>app</directory>
        </include>
    </source>
    <php>

        <env name="BCRYPT_ROUNDS" value="4"/>
        <env name="CACHE_DRIVER" value="array"/>
        <!-- <env name="DB_CONNECTION" value="sqlite"/> -->
        <!-- <env name="DB_DATABASE" value=":memory:"/> -->
        <env name="MAIL_MAILER" value="array"/>
        <env name="PULSE_ENABLED" value="false"/>
        <env name="QUEUE_CONNECTION" value="sync"/>
        <env name="SESSION_DRIVER" value="array"/>
        <env name="TELESCOPE_ENABLED" value="false"/>
    </php>
</phpunit>
```

### 48. `reproduce_dashboard_live.py`

```python
import re
import sys
import requests

BASE = "https://mycorner.site"
USERNAME = "admin"
PASSWORD = "Admin@123456"

session = requests.Session()
session.headers.update({"User-Agent": "Copilot-Debug/1.0"})

print("GET login page")
login_page = session.get(f"{BASE}/admin/login", timeout=20)
print("login page status:", login_page.status_code)

match = re.search(r'name="_token" value="([^"]+)"', login_page.text)
if not match:
    print("CSRF token not found")
    sys.exit(1)

token = match.group(1)
print("csrf token found")

login_resp = session.post(
    f"{BASE}/admin/login",
    data={
        "_token": token,
        "username": USERNAME,
        "password": PASSWORD,
    },
    allow_redirects=False,
    timeout=20,
)
print("login post status:", login_resp.status_code)
print("login redirect:", login_resp.headers.get("Location"))

page_resp = session.get(f"{BASE}/admin/dashboard", timeout=20)
print("dashboard page status:", page_resp.status_code)
print(page_resp.text[:800])

api_resp = session.get(
    f"{BASE}/api/realtime-dashboard",
    headers={
        "Accept": "application/json",
        "X-Requested-With": "XMLHttpRequest",
    },
    timeout=20,
)
print("api status:", api_resp.status_code)
print(api_resp.text[:2000])
```

### 49. `revert_drivers.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Revert to file driver (was working), check Redis config"""
import paramiko

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, t=30):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(t)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        if out: print(out[:600])
        if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower():
            print("ERR:", err[:300])
        return out

    print("[1] Check what Redis host Laravel is trying to use...")
    r("grep -E '^REDIS' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cat %s/config/database.php 2>/dev/null | grep -A5 'redis' | head -20" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[2] Check Laravel error log...")
    r("tail -30 %s/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null | grep -v '#[0-9]' | tail -15" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[3] Revert to file drivers (was working before)...")
    r("sed -i 's/CACHE_DRIVER=redis/CACHE_DRIVER=file/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("sed -i 's/SESSION_DRIVER=redis/SESSION_DRIVER=file/' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)

    r("grep -E '^(CACHE_DRIVER|SESSION_DRIVER|QUEUE_CONNECTION|REDIS)' %s/.env" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[4] Clear all caches...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, t=30)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, t=30)
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, t=30)
    r("cd %s && php artisan view:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH, t=30)

    print("\n[5] Final HTTP test...")
    out = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Admin/login: %{http_code}' http://localhost/admin/login")
    out2 = r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Main: %{http_code}' http://localhost/")

    if "200" in out or "302" in out2:
        print("\n[+] Application is WORKING!")
    else:
        print("\n[!] Still 500 - checking log...")
        r("tail -20 %s/storage/logs/laravel.log 2>/dev/null | grep -E 'ERROR|Exception|Error' | tail -5" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n===================================================")
    print("  http://%s/admin/login" % HOST)
    print("  Username: admin  |  Password: Admin@123456")
    print("===================================================")

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

```sql
-- MySQL Database Setup Script for Attendance Application
-- Run this on your VPS

-- Create database
CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS attendance_db CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

-- Create database user
CREATE USER IF NOT EXISTS 'attendance_user'@'localhost' IDENTIFIED BY 'SecurePassword123!';

-- Grant privileges
GRANT ALL PRIVILEGES ON attendance_db.* TO 'attendance_user'@'localhost';
FLUSH PRIVILEGES;

-- Verify
SHOW GRANTS FOR 'attendance_user'@'localhost';
```

```sql
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `personal_access_tokens` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
  `tokenable_type` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `tokenable_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `abilities` text NULL,
  `last_used_at` timestamp NULL,
  `expires_at` timestamp NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL
) DEFAULT CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
```

### 54. `update.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# Update Script for Attendance Application
# Use this to update your deployed Laravel application

set -e

APP_DIR="/var/www/attendance"
APP_USER="www-data"

echo "========================================"
echo "Updating Attendance Application"
echo "========================================"

cd $APP_DIR

# Backup database (recommended)
echo "Creating database backup..."
mysqldump -u attendance_user -pSecurePassword123! attendance_db > database_backup_$(date +%Y%m%d_%H%M%S).sql

# Pull latest code
echo "Pulling latest code from repository..."
sudo -u $APP_USER git pull origin main

# Install/update dependencies
echo "Installing composer dependencies..."
sudo -u $APP_USER composer install --optimize-autoloader --no-dev

# Update npm packages and rebuild assets
echo "Building frontend assets..."
sudo -u $APP_USER npm install
sudo -u $APP_USER npm run build

# Run migrations if any
echo "Running database migrations..."
php artisan migrate --force

# Clear caches
echo "Clearing application caches..."
php artisan optimize:clear
php artisan config:cache
php artisan route:cache
php artisan view:cache

# Restart services
echo "Restarting services..."
sudo systemctl restart php8.2-fpm nginx

echo ""
echo "========================================"
echo "Update completed successfully!"
echo "========================================"
```

### 55. `upload_kernel_fix.py`

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Upload Kernel.php fix and test the API"""
import paramiko
import io
import time

HOST = "187.77.173.160"
USERNAME = "root"
PASSWORD = "Goolbx512@@@@"
REMOTE_PATH = "/var/www/attendance"

def main():
    ssh = paramiko.SSHClient()
    ssh.set_missing_host_key_policy(paramiko.AutoAddPolicy())
    ssh.connect(HOST, username=USERNAME, password=PASSWORD, timeout=30)

    def r(cmd, t=30):
        i, o, e = ssh.exec_command(cmd)
        o.channel.settimeout(t)
        out = o.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        err = e.read().decode("utf-8", "ignore").strip()
        if out: print(out[:1000])
        if err and "warning" not in err.lower() and "deprecated" not in err.lower():
            print("ERR:", err[:400])
        return out

    print("[1] Uploading fixed Kernel.php...")
    sftp = ssh.open_sftp()
    with open(r"c:\Users\IT\Desktop\online_4-main\attendance-laravel\app\Http\Kernel.php", "rb") as f:
        sftp.putfo(f, REMOTE_PATH + "/app/Http/Kernel.php")
    sftp.close()
    print("[+] Kernel.php uploaded!")

    print("\n[2] Clearing and rebuilding caches...")
    r("cd %s && php artisan optimize:clear 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan config:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)
    r("cd %s && php artisan route:cache 2>&1" % REMOTE_PATH)

    print("\n[3] Login and test the API endpoint...")
    # Get login page + CSRF
    r("curl -s -c /tmp/cookies2.txt http://localhost/admin/login -o /tmp/lp.html")
    csrf = r("grep -oP '(?<=name=\"_token\" value=\")[^\"]+' /tmp/lp.html | head -1")
    print("CSRF:", csrf[:20] if csrf else "NOT FOUND")

    if csrf:
        # Get XSRF-TOKEN
        xsrf_raw = r("grep 'XSRF-TOKEN' /tmp/cookies2.txt | awk '{print $NF}' | head -1")
        # URL decode it
        xsrf = r("python3 -c \"import urllib.parse; print(urllib.parse.unquote('%s'))\" 2>/dev/null" % xsrf_raw)
        print("XSRF decoded:", xsrf[:30] if xsrf else "NOT FOUND")

        # POST login
        login_result = r("""curl -s \\
            -b /tmp/cookies2.txt \\
            -c /tmp/cookies2.txt \\
            -X POST http://localhost/admin/login \\
            -H 'Content-Type: application/x-www-form-urlencoded' \\
            -d '_token=%s&username=admin&password=Admin@123456' \\
            -w '\\nLogin status: %%{http_code}' \\
            -o /dev/null""" % csrf)

        # Test the realtime dashboard API
        print("\n[4] Testing /api/realtime-dashboard with session cookies...")
        result = r("""curl -s \\
            -b /tmp/cookies2.txt \\
            -H 'Accept: application/json' \\
            -H 'X-Requested-With: XMLHttpRequest' \\
            http://localhost/api/realtime-dashboard \\
            -w '\\nHTTP Status: %%{http_code}'""")

        if '"success":true' in result:
            print("\n[+] SUCCESS! API returning data correctly!")
        elif '"success":false' in result:
            print("\n[!] Still unauthorized - checking session...")
            r("cat /tmp/cookies2.txt")

    print("\n[5] Admin login page test...")
    r("curl -s -o /dev/null -w 'Admin page: %%{http_code}' http://localhost/admin/login")

    ssh.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

### 58. `app/Console/Kernel.php`

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console;

use Illuminate\Console\Scheduling\Schedule;
use Illuminate\Foundation\Console\Kernel as ConsoleKernel;

class Kernel extends ConsoleKernel
{
    /**
     * Define the application's command schedule.
     */
    protected function schedule(Schedule $schedule): void
    {
        $schedule->command('attendance:auto-checkout')->everyMinute();
        $schedule->command('notifications:send-reminders')->everyMinute();
        $schedule->command('backup:database')->dailyAt('02:00');
    }

    /**
     * Register the commands for the application.
     */
    protected function commands(): void
    {
        $this->load(__DIR__.'/Commands');

        require base_path('routes/console.php');
    }
}
```

---

### 59. `app/Console/Commands/AutoCheckout.php`

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use Illuminate\Console\Command;
use App\Models\Attendance;
use App\Models\Employee;
use App\Models\Branch;
use App\Services\ScheduleService;

class AutoCheckout extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'attendance:auto-checkout';
    protected $description = 'تسجيل انصراف تلقائي للموظفين الذين نسوا تسجيل الانصراف';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $today = today()->toDateString();
        $now   = now();

        // الموظفون الذين سجلوا دخول بدون انصراف
        $checkedInIds = Attendance::where('attendance_date', $today)
            ->where('type', 'in')
            ->pluck('employee_id')
            ->unique();

        $checkedOutIds = Attendance::where('attendance_date', $today)
            ->where('type', 'out')
            ->pluck('employee_id')
            ->unique();

        $pendingIds = $checkedInIds->diff($checkedOutIds);

        if ($pendingIds->isEmpty()) {
            $this->info('لا يوجد موظفين بحاجة لتسجيل انصراف تلقائي');
            return 0;
        }

        $count = 0;
        foreach ($pendingIds as $employeeId) {
            $employee = Employee::find($employeeId);
            if (!$employee) continue;

            $schedule = ScheduleService::getBranchSchedule($employee->branch_id);
            $coEndTime = $schedule['check_out_end_time'];

            $coEnd = strtotime($today . ' ' . $coEndTime);
            // Handle midnight crossing
            if ($coEnd < strtotime($today . ' ' . $schedule['check_in_start_time'])) {
                $coEnd = strtotime(today()->addDay()->toDateString() . ' ' . $coEndTime);
            }

            if ($now->timestamp >= $coEnd) {
                // Get last check-in location
                $lastCheckin = Attendance::where('employee_id', $employeeId)
                    ->where('attendance_date', $today)
                    ->where('type', 'in')
                    ->latest('timestamp')
                    ->first();

                Attendance::create([
                    'employee_id'     => $employeeId,
                    'type'            => 'out',
                    'timestamp'       => $now,
                    'attendance_date' => $today,
                    'late_minutes'    => 0,
                    'latitude'        => $lastCheckin->latitude ?? 0,
                    'longitude'       => $lastCheckin->longitude ?? 0,
                    'notes'           => 'تسجيل انصراف تلقائي',
                    'ip_address'      => '127.0.0.1',
                ]);

                $count++;
                $this->line("✅ تسجيل انصراف تلقائي: {$employee->name}");
            }
        }

        // إنهاء دوام إضافي مفتوح بعد الساعة 3 صباحاً
        if ((int) $now->format('H') >= 3) {
            $openOT = Attendance::where('attendance_date', $today)
                ->where('type', 'overtime-start')
                ->whereNotIn('employee_id', function ($q) use ($today) {
                    $q->select('employee_id')->from('attendances')
                        ->where('attendance_date', $today)
                        ->where('type', 'overtime-end');
                })
                ->get();

            foreach ($openOT as $ot) {
                Attendance::create([
                    'employee_id'     => $ot->employee_id,
                    'type'            => 'overtime-end',
                    'timestamp'       => $now,
                    'attendance_date' => $today,
                    'late_minutes'    => 0,
                    'latitude'        => $ot->latitude,
                    'longitude'       => $ot->longitude,
                    'notes'           => 'إنهاء دوام إضافي تلقائي',
                    'ip_address'      => '127.0.0.1',
                ]);
                $count++;
                $this->line("✅ إنهاء دوام إضافي تلقائي: الموظف #{$ot->employee_id}");
            }
        }

        $this->info("تم: {$count} عملية تلقائية");
        return 0;
    }
}
```

---

### 60. `app/Console/Commands/BackupDatabase.php`

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Services\BackupService;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;

class BackupDatabase extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'backup:database {--type=auto}';
    protected $description = 'إنشاء نسخة احتياطية لقاعدة البيانات';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $this->info('جاري إنشاء النسخة الاحتياطية...');

        $backup = BackupService::createDatabaseBackup($this->option('type'));

        if ($backup && $backup->status === 'completed') {
            $this->info("تم بنجاح: {$backup->filename} ({$backup->size_formatted})");
            return Command::SUCCESS;
        }

        $this->error('فشل إنشاء النسخة الاحتياطية: ' . ($backup?->notes ?? 'خطأ غير معروف'));
        return Command::FAILURE;
    }
}
```

---

### 61. `app/Console/Commands/SendReminders.php`

```php
<?php

namespace App\Console\Commands;

use App\Models\Employee;
use App\Models\Attendance;
use App\Models\Admin;
use App\Services\NotificationService;
use App\Services\ScheduleService;
use Illuminate\Console\Command;

class SendReminders extends Command
{
    protected $signature = 'notifications:send-reminders';
    protected $description = 'إرسال تذكيرات الحضور والتقارير اليومية';

    public function handle(): int
    {
        $this->sendAttendanceReminders();
        $this->sendDailySummary();

        $this->info('تم إرسال التذكيرات بنجاح');
        return Command::SUCCESS;
    }

    /**
     * تذكير الموظفين قبل 15 دقيقة من نهاية نافذة الحضور
     */
    private function sendAttendanceReminders(): void
    {
        $employees = Employee::active()->with('branch')->get();
        $today = today()->toDateString();

        foreach ($employees as $employee) {
            $schedule = ScheduleService::getBranchSchedule($employee->branch_id);
            $checkInEnd = $schedule['check_in_end_time'];

            // حساب الوقت المتبقي
            $endTime = strtotime($today . ' ' . $checkInEnd);
            $reminderTime = $endTime - (15 * 60); // 15 دقيقة قبل

            if (abs(time() - $reminderTime) > 120) { // نافذة ±2 دقيقة
                continue;
            }

            // تحقق: هل سجّل حضور اليوم؟
            $hasCheckedIn = Attendance::where('employee_id', $employee->id)
                ->where('attendance_date', $today)
                ->where('type', 'in')
                ->exists();

            if (!$hasCheckedIn) {
                NotificationService::notifyEmployee(
                    $employee->id,
                    'attendance_reminder',
                    'تذكير بالحضور',
                    "تبقى 15 دقيقة على نهاية نافذة الحضور ({$checkInEnd}). لم يتم تسجيل حضورك بعد."
                );
            }
        }
    }

    /**
     * إرسال تقرير يومي ملخص للمديرين
     */
    private function sendDailySummary(): void
    {
        $today = today()->toDateString();
        $now = now()->format('H:i');

        // إرسال الملخص في الساعة 17:00
        if ($now < '16:55' || $now > '17:10') {
            return;
        }

        $stats = Attendance::getTodayStats();
        $lateCount = Attendance::where('attendance_date', $today)
            ->where('type', 'in')
            ->where('late_minutes', '>', 0)
            ->count();

        $absentCount = $stats['total_employees'] - $stats['checked_in'];

        $body = "ملخص اليوم:\n";
        $body .= "• الحاضرون: {$stats['checked_in']}\n";
        $body .= "• المنصرفون: {$stats['checked_out']}\n";
        $body .= "• المتأخرون: {$lateCount}\n";
        $body .= "• الغائبون: {$absentCount}\n";
        $body .= "• إجمالي الموظفين: {$stats['total_employees']}";

        NotificationService::notifyAllAdmins(
            'daily_summary',
            'التقرير اليومي',
            $body,
            [
                'checked_in'  => $stats['checked_in'],
                'checked_out' => $stats['checked_out'],
                'late'        => $lateCount,
                'absent'      => $absentCount,
            ]
        );
    }
}
```

---

### 62. `app/Exceptions/Handler.php`

```php
<?php

namespace App\Exceptions;

use Illuminate\Foundation\Exceptions\Handler as ExceptionHandler;
use Throwable;

class Handler extends ExceptionHandler
{
    /**
     * The list of the inputs that are never flashed to the session on validation exceptions.
     *
     * @var array<int, string>
     */
    protected $dontFlash = [
        'current_password',
        'password',
        'password_confirmation',
    ];

    /**
     * Register the exception handling callbacks for the application.
     */
    public function register(): void
    {
        $this->reportable(function (Throwable $e) {
            //
        });
    }
}
```
